     9	export default function ConfirmationPage() {

    96	    <div className="mt-10 grid gap-6 lg:grid-cols-3">
    97	      {featuredPackages.map((item) => (
    98	        <PackagePreviewCard
    99	          key={item.id}
   100	          title={item.title}
   101	          duration={item.duration}
   102	          price={item.price}
   103	          image={item.image}
   104	          badge={item.badge}
   105	          highlights={item.highlights}
   106	        />
   107	      ))}
   108	    </div>
   109	  </div>
   110	</section>
   111	
   112	        <section className="py-16 sm:py-20 lg:py-24">
   113	          <div className="mx-auto max-w-7xl px-4 sm:px-6 lg:px-8">
   114	            <SectionHeading
   115	              eyebrow="Traveler Feedback"
   116	              title="Trusted by travelers who want a smoother planning experience."
   117	              description="Real feedback builds confidence. Keep the proof visible, calm, and premium."
   118	              align="center"
   119	            />
   120	
   121	            <div className="mt-10 grid gap-6 lg:grid-cols-3">
   122	              {featuredTestimonials.map((item) => (
   123	                <TestimonialCard
   124	                  key={item.id}
   125	                  name={item.name}
   126	                  role={item.role}
   127	                  quote={item.quote}
   128	                />
   129	              ))}
   130	            </div>
   131	          </div>
   132	        </section>
   133	
   134	                <section className="pb-16 pt-6 sm:pb-24">
   135	          <div className="mx-auto max-w-7xl px-4 sm:px-6 lg:px-8">
   136	            <div className="overflow-hidden rounded-[40px] border border-black/10 bg-[linear-gradient(135deg,#111827_0%,#1f2937_35%,#f97316_140%)] px-6 py-12 text-white shadow-[0_30px_120px_rgba(15,23,42,0.18)] sm:px-10 lg:px-14 lg:py-16">
   137	              <div className="max-w-2xl">
   138	                <p className="text-[11px] font-semibold uppercase tracking-[0.22em] text-orange-200">
   139	                  Start your journey
   140	                </p>
   141	                <h2 className="mt-4 text-3xl font-semibold tracking-tight sm:text-4xl">
   142	                  Ready to build a trip that feels more personalized from the start?
   143	                </h2>
   144	                <p className="mt-4 text-base leading-8 text-white/80">
   145	                  Begin with the trip builder, explore curated options, and move to
   146	                  review and confirmation with a flow that feels simple, clear, and
   147	                  premium throughout.
   148	                </p>
   149	
   150	                <div className="mt-8 flex flex-wrap gap-4">
   151	                  <a
   152	                    href="/trip-builder"
   153	                    className="inline-flex rounded-full bg-white px-6 py-3.5 text-sm font-semibold text-slate-950 transition hover:bg-slate-100"
   154	                  >
   155	                    Start Planning
   156	                  </a>
   157	                  <a
   158	                    href="/results"
   159	                    className="inline-flex rounded-full border border-white/20 bg-white/10 px-6 py-3.5 text-sm font-semibold text-white transition hover:bg-white/15"
   160	                  >
   161	                    Explore Trips
   162	                  </a>
   163	                </div>
   164	              </div>
   165	            </div>
   166	          </div>
   167	        </section>
   168	
   169	        <FaqSection />
   170	      </main>
   171	
   172	      <PublicFooter />
   173	    </div>
   174	  );

===== START: src/app/(public)/results/page.tsx =====
     1	"use client";
     2	
     3	import Link from "next/link";
     4	import { useRouter } from "next/navigation";
     5	import { PublicHeader } from "@/components/public/public-header";
     6	import { PublicFooter } from "@/components/public/public-footer";
     7	import { readyPackages } from "@/lib/mock/bangkok-builder-data";
     8	import { getRecommendedPackages } from "@/lib/helpers/recommendation";
     9	import { useTripBuilderStore } from "@/store/useTripBuilderStore";
    10	
    11	export default function ResultsPage() {
    12	  const router = useRouter();
    13	
    14	  const destination = useTripBuilderStore((state) => state.destination);
    15	  const segments = useTripBuilderStore((state) => state.segments);
    16	  const adults = useTripBuilderStore((state) => state.adults);
    17	  const children = useTripBuilderStore((state) => state.children);
    18	  const budget = useTripBuilderStore((state) => state.budget);
    19	  const travelStyle = useTripBuilderStore((state) => state.travelStyle);
    20	  const selectedPackageId = useTripBuilderStore((state) => state.selectedPackageId);
    21	  const selectPackage = useTripBuilderStore((state) => state.selectPackage);
    22	
    23	  const tripLabel = segments
    24	    .map((segment) => segment.city)
    25	    .filter(Boolean)
    26	    .join(" ŌåÆ ");
    27	
    28	  const recommendedPackages = getRecommendedPackages(
    29	    readyPackages.map((item, index) => ({
    30	      id: item.id,
    31	      title: item.title,
    32	      basePrice: item.price,
    33	      popularityScore: index === 0 ? 10 : 7 - index,
    34	      marginScore: item.hotelCategory === "4 Star" ? 8 : 7,
    35	      budgetFitScore:
    36	        budget === "Luxury"
    37	          ? item.price >= 40000
    38	            ? 9
    39	            : 5
    40	          : budget === "Premium"
    41	          ? item.price >= 30000 && item.price < 50000
    42	            ? 9
    43	            : 6
    44	          : budget === "Economy"
    45	          ? item.price < 32000
    46	            ? 9
    47	            : 5
    48	          : 8,
    49	      tripMoodFitScore:
    50	        travelStyle === "Mixed"
    51	          ? 8
    52	          : item.title.toLowerCase().includes(travelStyle.toLowerCase().split(" ")[0])
    53	          ? 9
    54	          : 6,
    55	      recommendedLabel: item.tag,
    56	    }))
    57	      .map((scored) => {
    58	        const original = readyPackages.find((pkg) => pkg.id === scored.id)!;
    59	        return {
    60	          ...original,
    61	          score: scored,
    62	        };
    63	      })
    64	      .sort((a, b) => {
    65	        const aScore =
    66	          (a.score.popularityScore || 0) +
    67	          (a.score.marginScore || 0) +
    68	          (a.score.budgetFitScore || 0) +
    69	          (a.score.tripMoodFitScore || 0);
    70	        const bScore =
    71	          (b.score.popularityScore || 0) +
    72	          (b.score.marginScore || 0) +
    73	          (b.score.budgetFitScore || 0) +
    74	          (b.score.tripMoodFitScore || 0);
    75	
    76	        return bScore - aScore;
    77	      })
    78	      .map((item) => item)
    79	  );
    80	
    81	  function handlePackageSelect(item: (typeof readyPackages)[number]) {
    82	    selectPackage({
    83	      selectedPackageId: item.id,
    84	      selectedPackageTitle: item.title,
    85	      selectedPackagePrice: item.price,
    86	    });
    87	
    88	    router.push("/customize");
    89	  }
    90	
    91	  return (
    92	    <div className="min-h-screen bg-[linear-gradient(180deg,#f8fbff_0%,#f8fafc_35%,#ffffff_100%)]">
    93	      <PublicHeader />
    94	
    95	      <main>
    96	        <section className="border-b border-slate-200/70 bg-white/60">
    97	          <div className="mx-auto max-w-7xl px-4 py-12 sm:px-6 lg:px-8">
    98	            <div className="rounded-[36px] border border-slate-200 bg-white p-6 shadow-[0_20px_70px_rgba(15,23,42,0.05)]">
    99	              <div className="flex flex-wrap items-center justify-between gap-4">
   100	                <div>
   101	                  <p className="text-sm font-medium text-sky-700">Results</p>
   102	                  <h1 className="mt-2 text-3xl font-semibold text-slate-950 sm:text-4xl">
   103	                    Curated options for your {destination} trip
   104	                  </h1>
   105	                  <p className="mt-3 text-sm text-slate-600">
   106	                    {tripLabel || destination} ŌĆó {adults} Adults
   107	                    {children ? `, ${children} Children` : ""} ŌĆó {travelStyle}
   108	                  </p>
   109	                </div>
   110	
   111	                <div className="flex flex-wrap gap-3">
   112	                  <Link
   113	                    href="/trip-builder"
   114	                    className="rounded-2xl border border-slate-200 bg-white px-5 py-3 text-sm font-semibold text-slate-800 transition hover:bg-slate-50"
   115	                  >
   116	                    Edit Search
   117	                  </Link>
   118	
   119	                  {selectedPackageId ? (
   120	                    <Link
   121	                      href="/customize"
   122	                      className="rounded-2xl bg-slate-950 px-5 py-3 text-sm font-semibold text-white transition hover:bg-slate-800"
   123	                    >
   124	                      Continue to Customize
   125	                    </Link>
   126	                  ) : null}
   127	                </div>
   128	              </div>
   129	
   130	              <div className="mt-6 flex flex-wrap gap-3">
   131	                {[
   132	                  `Budget: ${budget}`,
   133	                  "Package-led recommendations",
   134	                  "Custom edits available next",
   135	                ].map((item) => (
   136	                  <span
   137	                    key={item}
   138	                    className="rounded-full border border-sky-200 bg-sky-50 px-3 py-1.5 text-xs font-semibold text-sky-700"
   139	                  >
   140	                    {item}
   141	                  </span>
   142	                ))}
   143	              </div>
   144	            </div>
   145	          </div>
   146	        </section>
   147	
   148	        <section className="mx-auto max-w-7xl px-4 py-10 sm:px-6 lg:px-8 lg:py-14">
   149	          <div className="grid gap-8 lg:grid-cols-[300px_1fr]">
   150	            <aside className="space-y-6">
   151	              <div className="rounded-[36px] border border-slate-200 bg-white p-6 shadow-[0_20px_70px_rgba(15,23,42,0.05)]">
   152	                <h2 className="text-lg font-semibold text-slate-950">Trip Filters</h2>
   153	                <div className="mt-5 space-y-4 text-sm">
   154	                  {[
   155	                    `Budget: ${budget}`,
   156	                    `Style: ${travelStyle}`,
   157	                    `Travellers: ${adults + children}`,
   158	                    tripLabel ? `Route: ${tripLabel}` : "Route: Bangkok",
   159	                  ].map((item) => (
   160	                    <div
   161	                      key={item}
   162	                      className="rounded-2xl bg-slate-50 px-4 py-3 text-slate-700"
   163	                    >
   164	                      {item}
   165	                    </div>
   166	                  ))}
   167	                </div>
   168	              </div>
   169	
   170	              <div className="rounded-[36px] border border-slate-200 bg-white p-6 shadow-[0_20px_70px_rgba(15,23,42,0.05)]">
   171	                <p className="text-sm font-medium text-sky-700">Planning Note</p>
   172	                <p className="mt-3 text-sm leading-7 text-slate-600">
   173	                  Select a package to continue. In the next step you can refine room preference,
   174	                  extras, and trip-level choices before review.
   175	                </p>
   176	              </div>
   177	            </aside>
   178	
   179	            <section className="space-y-6">
   180	              {recommendedPackages.map((item) => {
   181	                const isSelected = selectedPackageId === item.id;
   182	
   183	                return (
   184	                  <div
   185	                    key={item.id}
   186	                    className={`overflow-hidden rounded-[36px] border bg-white shadow-[0_20px_70px_rgba(15,23,42,0.06)] transition ${
   187	                      isSelected ? "border-sky-300 ring-2 ring-sky-100" : "border-slate-200"
   188	                    }`}
   189	                  >
   190	                    <div className="grid gap-0 xl:grid-cols-[1.1fr_0.9fr]">
   191	                      <div className="p-6 sm:p-8">
   192	                        <div className="flex flex-wrap items-center gap-3">
   193	                          <span className="inline-flex rounded-full border border-sky-200 bg-sky-50 px-3 py-1 text-xs font-semibold text-sky-700">
   194	                            {item.tag}
   195	                          </span>
   196	                          {isSelected ? (
   197	                            <span className="inline-flex rounded-full border border-emerald-200 bg-emerald-50 px-3 py-1 text-xs font-semibold text-emerald-700">
   198	                              Selected
   199	                            </span>
   200	                          ) : null}
   201	                        </div>
   202	
   203	                        <h2 className="mt-4 text-2xl font-semibold text-slate-950 sm:text-3xl">
   204	                          {item.title}
   205	                        </h2>
   206	
   207	                        <div className="mt-5 grid gap-3 sm:grid-cols-3">
   208	                          <div className="rounded-2xl bg-slate-50 px-4 py-3 text-sm text-slate-700">
   209	                            {item.nights} Nights
   210	                          </div>
   211	                          <div className="rounded-2xl bg-slate-50 px-4 py-3 text-sm text-slate-700">
   212	                            {item.hotelCategory}
   213	                          </div>
   214	                          <div className="rounded-2xl bg-slate-50 px-4 py-3 text-sm text-slate-700">
   215	                            {item.area}
   216	                          </div>
   217	                        </div>
   218	
   219	                        <div className="mt-6 flex flex-wrap gap-3">
   220	                          {item.includes.map((tag) => (
   221	                            <span

===== START: src/app/(public)/review/page.tsx =====
     1	"use client";
     2	
     3	import Link from "next/link";
     4	import { PublicHeader } from "@/components/public/public-header";
     5	import { PublicFooter } from "@/components/public/public-footer";
     6	import { useTripBuilderStore } from "@/store/useTripBuilderStore";
     7	
     8	export default function ReviewPage() {
     9	  const selectedPackageTitle = useTripBuilderStore((state) => state.selectedPackageTitle);
    10	  const selectedPackagePrice = useTripBuilderStore((state) => state.selectedPackagePrice);
    11	  const adults = useTripBuilderStore((state) => state.adults);
    12	  const children = useTripBuilderStore((state) => state.children);
    13	  const roomPreference = useTripBuilderStore((state) => state.roomPreference);
    14	  const serviceFee = useTripBuilderStore((state) => state.serviceFee);
    15	  const bookingId = useTripBuilderStore((state) => state.bookingId);
    16	  const selectedExtras = useTripBuilderStore((state) => state.selectedExtras);
    17	  const estimatedHotelTotal = useTripBuilderStore((state) => state.estimatedHotelTotal);
    18	  const estimatedTransferTotal = useTripBuilderStore((state) => state.estimatedTransferTotal);
    19	  const estimatedSightseeingTotal = useTripBuilderStore((state) => state.estimatedSightseeingTotal);
    20	  const estimatedMealsTotal = useTripBuilderStore((state) => state.estimatedMealsTotal);
    21	  const estimatedGrandTotal = useTripBuilderStore((state) => state.estimatedGrandTotal);
    22	
    23	  const fallbackExtrasTotal = selectedExtras.length * 900;
    24	  const finalPrice =
    25	    estimatedGrandTotal > 0
    26	      ? estimatedGrandTotal
    27	      : selectedPackagePrice + fallbackExtrasTotal + serviceFee;
    28	
    29	  return (
    30	    <div className="min-h-screen bg-[linear-gradient(180deg,#f8fbff_0%,#f8fafc_35%,#ffffff_100%)]">
    31	      <PublicHeader />
    32	
    33	      <main>
    34	        <section className="border-b border-slate-200/70 bg-white/60">
    35	          <div className="mx-auto max-w-7xl px-4 py-14 sm:px-6 lg:px-8">
    36	            <div className="max-w-3xl">
    37	              <span className="inline-flex rounded-full border border-sky-200 bg-sky-50 px-3 py-1 text-[11px] font-semibold uppercase tracking-[0.22em] text-sky-700">
    38	                Review
    39	              </span>
    40	              <h1 className="mt-4 text-4xl font-semibold tracking-tight text-slate-950 sm:text-5xl">
    41	                Review your trip before confirming.
    42	              </h1>
    43	              <p className="mt-4 text-base leading-8 text-slate-600 sm:text-lg">
    44	                Check your selected trip details, useful extras, and current final estimate before confirmation.
    45	              </p>
    46	            </div>
    47	          </div>
    48	        </section>
    49	
    50	        <section className="mx-auto max-w-7xl px-4 py-10 sm:px-6 lg:px-8 lg:py-14">
    51	          <div className="grid gap-8 xl:grid-cols-[1.05fr_0.95fr]">
    52	            <section className="rounded-[36px] border border-slate-200 bg-white p-6 shadow-[0_20px_70px_rgba(15,23,42,0.06)] sm:p-8">
    53	              <div>
    54	                <h2 className="text-2xl font-semibold text-slate-950">
    55	                  {selectedPackageTitle || "Selected trip"}
    56	                </h2>
    57	                <p className="mt-2 text-sm text-slate-600">
    58	                  {adults} Adults{children ? `, ${children} Children` : ""} ŌĆó {roomPreference} ŌĆó Review summary
    59	                </p>
    60	              </div>
    61	
    62	              <div className="mt-8 grid gap-4 sm:grid-cols-2">
    63	                <div className="rounded-[24px] bg-slate-50 p-5">
    64	                  <p className="text-sm font-medium text-slate-500">Stay</p>
    65	                  <p className="mt-2 font-semibold text-slate-950">
    66	                    Ōé╣{estimatedHotelTotal.toLocaleString("en-IN")} hotel estimate
    67	                  </p>
    68	                </div>
    69	
    70	                <div className="rounded-[24px] bg-slate-50 p-5">
    71	                  <p className="text-sm font-medium text-slate-500">Transfers</p>
    72	                  <p className="mt-2 font-semibold text-slate-950">
    73	                    Ōé╣{estimatedTransferTotal.toLocaleString("en-IN")} movement estimate
    74	                  </p>
    75	                </div>
    76	
    77	                <div className="rounded-[24px] bg-slate-50 p-5">
    78	                  <p className="text-sm font-medium text-slate-500">Room Preference</p>
    79	                  <p className="mt-2 font-semibold text-slate-950">{roomPreference}</p>
    80	                </div>
    81	
    82	                <div className="rounded-[24px] bg-slate-50 p-5">
    83	                  <p className="text-sm font-medium text-slate-500">Travelers</p>
    84	                  <p className="mt-2 font-semibold text-slate-950">
    85	                    {adults} Adults{children ? `, ${children} Children` : ""}
    86	                  </p>
    87	                </div>
    88

    90	                  <p className="text-sm font-medium text-slate-500">Selected Extras</p>
    91	                  <div className="mt-3 flex flex-wrap gap-2">
    92	                    {selectedExtras.length > 0 ? (
    93	                      selectedExtras.map((item) => (
    94	                        <span
    95	                          key={item}
    96	                          className="rounded-full bg-white px-3 py-1 text-xs font-medium text-slate-700 ring-1 ring-slate-200"
    97	                        >
    98	                          {item}
    99	                        </span>
   100	                      ))
   101	                    ) : (
   102	                      <p className="text-sm font-medium text-slate-950">
   103	                        No extras selected
   104	                      </p>
   105	                    )}
   106	                  </div>
   107	                </div>
   108	
   109	                <div className="rounded-[24px] bg-slate-50 p-5 sm:col-span-2">
   110	                  <p className="text-sm font-medium text-slate-500">Experiences & meals</p>
   111	                  <p className="mt-2 font-semibold text-slate-950">
   112	                    Ōé╣{estimatedSightseeingTotal.toLocaleString("en-IN")} sightseeing ŌĆó Ōé╣
   113	                    {Math.max(estimatedMealsTotal, fallbackExtrasTotal).toLocaleString("en-IN")} meals/extras
   114	                  </p>
   115	                </div>
   116	              </div>
   117	
   118	              <div className="mt-8 rounded-[28px] border border-slate-200 p-5">
   119	                <h3 className="text-base font-semibold text-slate-950">Booking Summary</h3>
   120	                <p className="mt-3 text-sm leading-7 text-slate-600">
   121	                  This review is now tied to your central trip engine totals, so selections made in
   122	                  earlier steps carry through more consistently into confirmation.
   123	                </p>
   124	              </div>
   125	            </section>
   126	
   127	            <aside className="space-y-6">
   128	              <div className="rounded-[36px] border border-slate-200 bg-white p-6 shadow-[0_20px_70px_rgba(15,23,42,0.05)]">
   129	                <h2 className="text-lg font-semibold text-slate-950">Price Summary</h2>
   130	                <div className="mt-5 space-y-4 text-sm">
   131	                  <div className="flex justify-between">
   132	                    <span className="text-slate-500">Package base</span>
   133	                    <span className="font-medium text-slate-950">
   134	                      Ōé╣{selectedPackagePrice.toLocaleString("en-IN")}
   135	                    </span>
   136	                  </div>

===== START: src/components/public/ai-helper-widget.tsx =====
     1	"use client";
     2	
     3	import { useEffect, useMemo, useState } from "react";
     4	import { Search, Sparkles, Wand2 } from "lucide-react";
     5	
     6	const prompts = [
     7	  "Plan your next dream vacation...",
     8	  "Where do you want to go?",
     9	  "Type your destination...",
    10	  "Find your perfect getaway...",
    11	  "Let AI help you plan faster...",
    12	];
    13	
    14	type AiHelperWidgetProps = {
    15	  className?: string;
    16	  compact?: boolean;
    17	};
    18	
    19	export function AiHelperWidget({
    20	  className = "",
    21	  compact = false,
    22	}: AiHelperWidgetProps) {
    23	  const [activeIndex, setActiveIndex] = useState(0);
    24	  const [displayedText, setDisplayedText] = useState("");
    25	  const activePrompt = useMemo(() => prompts[activeIndex], [activeIndex]);
    26	
    27	  useEffect(() => {
    28	    let current = 0;
    29	    setDisplayedText("");
    30	
    31	    const typingInterval = setInterval(() => {
    32	      current += 1;
    33	      setDisplayedText(activePrompt.slice(0, current));
    34	
    35	      if (current >= activePrompt.length) {
    36	        clearInterval(typingInterval);
    37	      }
    38	    }, 30);
    39	
    40	    return () => clearInterval(typingInterval);
    41	  }, [activePrompt]);
    42	
    43	  useEffect(() => {
    44	    const interval = setInterval(() => {
    45	      setActiveIndex((prev) => (prev + 1) % prompts.length);
    46	    }, 2600);
    47	
    48	    return () => clearInterval(interval);
    49	  }, []);
    50	
    51	  return (
    52	    <div
    53	      className={`ai-widget-shell group relative overflow-hidden rounded-[18px] p-[1.5px] ${
    54	        compact ? "min-h-[54px]" : "min-h-[72px]"
    55	      } ${className}`}
    56	    >
    57	      <div className="ai-widget-inner relative h-full rounded-[16px] bg-[linear-gradient(135deg,rgba(255,255,255,0.97),rgba(248,250,252,0.94))] px-3 py-2 backdrop-blur-xl sm:px-4">
    58	        <div className="pointer-events-none absolute inset-0 rounded-[16px] bg-[radial-gradient(circle_at_top_left,rgba(255,255,255,0.95),transparent_34%),radial-gradient(circle_at_bottom_right,rgba(59,130,246,0.10),transparent_36%)]" />
    59	        <div className="ai-widget-shine pointer-events-none absolute -left-20 top-0 h-full w-16 rotate-12 bg-white/50 blur-xl" />
    60	
    61	        <div className="relative z-10 flex items-center gap-2">
    62	          <div className="relative flex h-7 w-7 shrink-0 items-center justify-center rounded-xl bg-slate-950 text-white shadow-[0_8px_18px_rgba(15,23,42,0.18)] sm:h-8 sm:w-8">
    63	            <div className="absolute inset-0 rounded-xl bg-sky-400/25 blur-md animate-pulse" />
    64	            <Sparkles className="relative h-3.5 w-3.5 animate-pulse" />
    65	          </div>
    66	
    67	          <div className="min-w-0 flex-1">
    68	            <div className="mb-0.5 flex items-center gap-2">
    69	              <span className="inline-flex items-center gap-1 rounded-full bg-sky-50 px-2 py-0.5 text-[8px] font-semibold uppercase tracking-[0.2em] text-sky-700">
    70	                <Wand2 className="h-2.5 w-2.5" />
    71	                AI Trip Assist
    72	              </span>

   114	export function FaqSection() {
   115	  const [activeGroup, setActiveGroup] = useState(faqGroups[0].key);
   116	  const currentGroup =
   117	    faqGroups.find((group) => group.key === activeGroup) ?? faqGroups[0];
   118	
   119	  const initialOpen = useMemo(() => currentGroup.faqs[0]?.question ?? "", [currentGroup]);
   120	  const [openQuestion, setOpenQuestion] = useState(initialOpen);
   121	
   122	  if (openQuestion !== initialOpen && !currentGroup.faqs.some((faq) => faq.question === openQuestion)) {
   123	    setOpenQuestion(initialOpen);
   124	  }
   125	
   126	  return (
   127	    <section className="py-16 sm:py-20 lg:py-24">
   128	      <div className="mx-auto max-w-7xl px-4 sm:px-6 lg:px-8">
   129	        <div className="relative overflow-hidden rounded-[36px] border border-slate-200 bg-[linear-gradient(135deg,rgba(255,247,247,0.95)_0%,rgba(243,247,255,0.94)_45%,rgba(232,250,255,0.96)_100%)] p-6 shadow-[0_24px_80px_rgba(15,23,42,0.06)] sm:p-8 lg:p-12">
   130	          <div className="pointer-events-none absolute inset-0 bg-[radial-gradient(circle_at_18%_72%,rgba(251,146,60,0.10),transparent_22%),radial-gradient(circle_at_78%_26%,rgba(56,189,248,0.12),transparent_24%),radial-gradient(circle_at_50%_88%,rgba(167,139,250,0.10),transparent_18%)]" />

   136	
   137	          <div className="relative">
   138	            <div className="mx-auto max-w-3xl text-center">
   139	              <span className="inline-flex rounded-full border border-slate-200 bg-white/70 px-3 py-1 text-[10px] font-semibold uppercase tracking-[0.22em] text-slate-600">

   141	              </span>

   157

     1	import Link from "next/link";

     4	type HeroSearchCardProps = {

===== START: src/components/public/live-price-sidebar.tsx =====
     1	import { Wallet, ArrowUpRight, BadgeIndianRupee } from "lucide-react";
     2	import { formatCurrency } from "@/lib/helpers/format";
     3	
     4	type LivePriceSidebarProps = {
     5	  selectedPackagePrice: number;
     6	  serviceFee: number;
     7	  travelStyle: string;
     8	};
     9	
    10	function getPlanningMultiplier(travelStyle: string) {
    11	  const value = travelStyle.toLowerCase();
    12	
    13	  if (value.includes("luxury")) return 1.28;
    14	  if (value.includes("honeymoon")) return 1.18;
    15	  if (value.includes("family")) return 1.12;
    16	  if (value.includes("adventure")) return 1.1;
    17	  if (value.includes("budget")) return 0.92;
    18	
    19	  return 1;
    20	}
    21	
    22	export function LivePriceSidebar({
    23	  selectedPackagePrice,
    24	  serviceFee,
    25	  travelStyle,
    26	}: LivePriceSidebarProps) {
    27	  const styleMultiplier = getPlanningMultiplier(travelStyle);
    28	  const planningEstimate = Math.round(selectedPackagePrice * styleMultiplier);
    29	  const estimatedTotal = planningEstimate + serviceFee;
    30	
    31	  return (
    32	    <div className="overflow-hidden rounded-[30px] border border-slate-200 bg-white shadow-[0_20px_50px_rgba(15,23,42,0.06)]">
    33	      <div className="bg-[linear-gradient(135deg,#0f172a_0%,#1d4ed8_100%)] p-5 text-white sm:p-6">
    34	        <div className="flex items-start justify-between gap-3">
    35	          <div>
    36	            <p className="text-[11px] font-semibold uppercase tracking-[0.22em] text-white/70">
    37	              Planning Estimate
    38	            </p>
    39	            <h3 className="mt-2 text-2xl font-semibold tracking-tight">
    40	              {formatCurrency(estimatedTotal)}
    41	            </h3>
    42	            <p className="mt-2 text-sm leading-6 text-white/80">
    43	              Early estimate based on your current trip style and saved base package.
    44	            </p>
    45	          </div>
    46	
    47	          <span className="inline-flex h-11 w-11 items-center justify-center rounded-2xl bg-white/10">
    48	            <Wallet className="h-5 w-5" />
    49	          </span>
    50	        </div>
    51	      </div>
    52	
    53	      <div className="space-y-4 p-5 sm:p-6">
    54	        <div className="flex items-center justify-between text-sm">
    55	          <span className="text-slate-500">Saved base package</span>
    56	          <span className="font-semibold text-slate-900">
    57	            {formatCurrency(selectedPackagePrice)}
    58	          </span>
    59	        </div>
    60	
    61	        <div className="flex items-center justify-between text-sm">
    62	          <span className="text-slate-500">Style-led planning impact</span>
    63	          <span className="font-semibold text-slate-900">
    64	            {formatCurrency(planningEstimate - selectedPackagePrice)}
    65	          </span>
    66	        </div>
    67	
    68	        <div className="flex items-center justify-between text-sm">
    69	          <span className="text-slate-500">Service fee</span>
    70	          <span className="font-semibold text-slate-900">
    71	            {formatCurrency(serviceFee)}
    72	          </span>
    73	        </div>
    74	
    75	        <div className="rounded-[22px] bg-slate-50 p-4">
    76	          <div className="flex items-start gap-3">
    77	            <span className="inline-flex h-10 w-10 items-center justify-center rounded-2xl bg-white text-slate-700 shadow-sm">
    78	              <BadgeIndianRupee className="h-4 w-4" />
    79	            </span>
    80	            <div>
    81	              <p className="text-sm font-semibold text-slate-900">
    82	                Better-fit options will show next
    83	              </p>
    84	              <p className="mt-1 text-sm leading-6 text-slate-600">
    85	                In Results, weŌĆÖll prioritize stronger-fit packages, best-value picks,
    86	                and worthwhile upgrades instead of dumping random options.
    87	              </p>
    88	            </div>

===== START: src/components/public/public-header.tsx =====
     1	"use client";
     2	
     3	import Link from "next/link";
     4	import { useEffect, useRef, useState } from "react";
     5	
     6	const navItems = [
     7	  { label: "Destinations", href: "/results" },
     8	  { label: "Packages", href: "/results" },
     9	  { label: "Plan Your Trip", href: "/trip-builder" },
    10	  { label: "Contact", href: "/" },
    11	];
    12	
    13	export function PublicHeader() {
    14	  const [visible, setVisible] = useState(true);
    15	  const lastY = useRef(0);
    16	
    17	  useEffect(() => {
    18	    const onScroll = () => {
    19	      const currentY = window.scrollY;
    20	
    21	      if (currentY < 20) {
    22	        setVisible(true);
    23	        lastY.current = currentY;
    24	        return;
    25	      }
    26	
    27	      if (currentY > lastY.current && currentY > 80) {
    28	        setVisible(false);
    29	      } else {
    30	        setVisible(true);
    31	      }
    32	
    33	      lastY.current = currentY;
    34	    };
    35	
    36	    window.addEventListener("scroll", onScroll, { passive: true });
    37	    return () => window.removeEventListener("scroll", onScroll);
    38	  }, []);
    39	
    40	  return (
    41	    <header
    42	      className={`fixed inset-x-0 top-3 z-[70] px-3 transition-all duration-300 sm:top-5 sm:px-5 ${
    43	        visible
    44	          ? "translate-y-0 opacity-100"
    45	          : "-translate-y-5 pointer-events-none opacity-0"
    46	      }`}
    47	    >
    48	      <div className="mx-auto max-w-7xl">
    49	        <div className="flex items-center justify-between rounded-[30px] bg-[#f6f1e8]/72 px-4 py-3 backdrop-blur-xl sm:px-6">
    50	          <Link href="/" className="flex items-center gap-3">
    51	            <div className="flex h-10 w-10 items-center justify-center rounded-2xl bg-[linear-gradient(135deg,#0f172a_0%,#f97316_100%)] text-xs font-bold text-white shadow-[0_10px_24px_rgba(15,23,42,0.18)]">
    52	              ET
    53	            </div>
    54	            <div>
    55	              <p className="text-[11px] font-semibold tracking-[0.18em] text-slate-900 sm:text-xs">
    56	                EASYTRIP365
    57	              </p>
    58	              <p className="text-[10px] text-slate-500 sm:text-xs">
    59	                Curated holiday journeys
    60	              </p>
    61	            </div>
    62	          </Link>
    63	
    64	          <nav className="hidden items-center gap-3 lg:flex">
    65	            {navItems.map((item) => (
    66	              <Link
    67	                key={item.label}
    68	                href={item.href}
    69	                className="rounded-full border border-black/70 bg-transparent px-5 py-2.5 text-sm font-medium text-slate-800 transition hover:border-black hover:text-slate-950"
    70	              >
    71	                {item.label}
    72	              </Link>
    73	            ))}
    74	          </nav>
    75	
    76	          <Link
    77	            href="/trip-builder"
    78	            className="inline-flex rounded-full bg-orange-500 px-5 py-2.5 text-sm font-semibold text-white shadow-[0_14px_30px_rgba(249,115,22,0.28)] transition hover:bg-orange-600"
    79	          >
    80	            Start Planning
    81	          </Link>
    82	        </div>
    83	      </div>
    84	    </header>
    85	  );
    86	}

     1	const travelStyleOptions = [
     2	  "Leisure",
     3	  "Premium Leisure",
     4	  "Luxury Escape",
     5	  "Fast-Paced Explorer",
     6	];
     7

     9	  value: string;
    10	  onChange?: (value: string) => void;

    13	export function TravelStyleSelector({
    14	  value,
    15	  onChange,
    16	}: TravelStyleSelectorProps) {
    17	  return (
    18	    <div className="grid gap-3 md:grid-cols-2">

    24	            key={option}
    25	            type="button"
    26	            onClick={() => onChange?.(option)}
    27	            className={`rounded-3xl border p-4 text-left transition ${
    28	              active
    29	                ? "border-black bg-black text-white"
    30	                : "border-neutral-200 bg-white text-neutral-900 hover:border-neutral-400"
    31	            }`}
    32	          >
    33	            <p className="text-sm font-bold">{option}</p>
    34	          </button>
    35	        );
    36	      })}

===== START: src/components/public/trip-builder-stepper.tsx =====
     1	type TripBuilderStepperProps = {
     2	  currentStep: number;
     3	};
     4	
     5	const steps = [
     6	  { number: "01", label: "Choose" },
     7	  { number: "02", label: "Results" },
     8	  { number: "03", label: "Customize" },
     9	  { number: "04", label: "Review" },
    10	  { number: "05", label: "Confirm" },
    11	];
    12	
    13	export function TripBuilderStepper({
    14	  currentStep,
    15	}: TripBuilderStepperProps) {
    16	  return (
    17	    <div className="rounded-[28px] border border-white/70 bg-white/75 p-3 shadow-[0_18px_50px_rgba(15,23,42,0.06)] backdrop-blur">
    18	      <div className="grid gap-2 md:grid-cols-5">
    19	        {steps.map((step, index) => {
    20	          const stepNumber = index + 1;
    21	          const isActive = stepNumber === currentStep;
    22	          const isComplete = stepNumber < currentStep;
    23	
    24	          return (
    25	            <div
    26	              key={step.label}
    27	              className={`rounded-[22px] border px-4 py-3 transition ${
    28	                isActive
    29	                  ? "border-slate-950 bg-slate-950 text-white shadow-[0_16px_34px_rgba(15,23,42,0.20)]"
    30	                  : isComplete
    31	                  ? "border-emerald-200 bg-emerald-50 text-emerald-800"
    32	                  : "border-slate-200 bg-white text-slate-500"
    33	              }`}
    34	            >
    35	              <p
    36	                className={`text-[11px] font-semibold uppercase tracking-[0.22em] ${
    37	                  isActive ? "text-white/70" : isComplete ? "text-emerald-600" : "text-slate-400"
    38	                }`}
    39	              >
    40	                {step.number}
    41	              </p>
    42	              <p className="mt-1 text-sm font-semibold">{step.label}</p>
    43	            </div>
    44	          );
    45	        })}
    46	      </div>
    47	    </div>
    48	  );
    49	}===== END: src/components/public/trip-builder-stepper.tsx =====

    77	export function WhyChooseUsGrid() {
    78	  const sectionRef = useRef<HTMLElement | null>(null);
    79	  const [isOpen, setIsOpen] = useState(false);
    80	
    81	  useEffect(() => {
    82	    const node = sectionRef.current;
    83	    if (!node) return;
    84	
    85	    const observer = new IntersectionObserver(
    86	      ([entry]) => {
    87	        setIsOpen(entry.isIntersecting && entry.intersectionRatio > 0.42);
    88	      },
    89	      {
    90	        threshold: [0.2, 0.42, 0.6],
    91	      }
    92	    );
    93	
    94	    observer.observe(node);
    95	    return () => observer.disconnect();
    96	  }, []);
    97	
    98	  return (
    99	    <section
   100	      ref={sectionRef}
   101	      className="overflow-hidden rounded-[34px] border border-slate-200 bg-[linear-gradient(180deg,#f7fbfb_0%,#eff5f4_55%,#f7f7f4_100%)] px-4 py-8 shadow-[0_20px_60px_rgba(15,23,42,0.06)] sm:px-6 sm:py-10 lg:px-8 lg:py-12"
   102	    >
   103	      <div className="mx-auto max-w-6xl">
   104	        <div className="text-center">

     3	type BadgeVariant = "default" | "success" | "warning" | "premium" | "muted";
     4	
     5	type BadgeProps = {
     6	  children: ReactNode;
     7	  variant?: BadgeVariant;
     8	  className?: string;
     9	};
    10	
    11	const variantClasses: Record<BadgeVariant, string> = {
    12	  default: "bg-slate-100 text-slate-700",
    13	  success: "bg-emerald-100 text-emerald-700",
    14	  warning: "bg-amber-100 text-amber-700",
    15	  premium: "bg-purple-100 text-purple-700",
    16	  muted: "bg-slate-200 text-slate-600",
    17	};
    18	
    19	export function Badge({
    20	  children,
    21	  variant = "default",
    22	  className = "",
    23	}: BadgeProps) {
    24	  return (
    25	    <span
    26	      className={`inline-flex items-center rounded-full px-3 py-1 text-xs font-semibold ${variantClasses[variant]} ${className}`}
    27	    >
    28	      {children}
    29	    </span>
    30	  );

===== START: src/components/trip-builder/ai-guided-flow.tsx =====
     1	"use client";
     2	
     3	type AIGuidedFlowProps = {
     4	  tripStyle?: string;
     5	  travellingWith?: string;
     6	  budget?: string;
     7	  priority?: string;
     8	  specialRequest?: string;
     9	};
    10	
    11	function normalize(value: string | undefined, fallback: string) {
    12	  return (value ?? fallback).toLowerCase();
    13	}
    14	
    15	function getRecommendation(params: {
    16	  tripStyle?: string;
    17	  travellingWith?: string;
    18	  budget?: string;
    19	  priority?: string;
    20	  specialRequest?: string;
    21	}) {
    22	  const style = normalize(params.tripStyle, "mixed");
    23	  const group = normalize(params.travellingWith, "couple");
    24	  const budget = normalize(params.budget, "comfort");
    25	  const priority = normalize(params.priority, "value");
    26	  const specialRequest = params.specialRequest?.trim() ?? "";
    27	
    28	  let title = "Balanced Thailand Plan";
    29	  let summary =
    30	    "A well-paced Thailand itinerary with a practical mix of comfort, sightseeing, and free time.";
    31	  let hotelTier = "4Ōśģ hotel";
    32	  let route = "Bangkok + Pattaya";
    33	  let nights = "5N / 6D";
    34	
    35	  if (style.includes("luxury")) {
    36	    title = "Luxury Thailand Escape";
    37	    summary =
    38	      "Premium stay selection with smoother transfers, elevated hotel comfort, and slower pacing.";
    39	    hotelTier = "4Ōśģ premium stay";
    40	    route = "Bangkok + Pattaya";
    41	    nights = "5N / 6D";
    42	  } else if (style.includes("shopping")) {
    43	    title = "Bangkok Shopping Break";
    44	    summary =
    45	      "Built around city convenience, shopping zones, easy transfers, and flexible evenings.";
    46	    hotelTier = "4Ōśģ city hotel";
    47	    route = "Bangkok";
    48	    nights = "4N / 5D";
    49	  } else if (style.includes("nightlife")) {
    50	    title = "Bangkok After Dark";
    51	    summary =
    52	      "A city-led plan with late evenings, central stays, and flexible daytime recovery windows.";
    53	    hotelTier = "4Ōśģ central stay";
    54	    route = "Bangkok + Pattaya";
    55	    nights = "4N / 5D";
    56	  } else if (style.includes("family")) {
    57	    title = "Family Fun Thailand";
    58	    summary =
    59	      "A smoother itinerary with practical transfers, family-friendly pacing, and lighter day loads.";
    60	    hotelTier = "4Ōśģ family-friendly hotel";
    61	    route = "Bangkok + Pattaya";
    62	    nights = "5N / 6D";
    63	  } else if (style.includes("adventure")) {
    64	    title = "Adventure Thailand Route";
    65	    summary =
    66	      "An active trip structure with day outings, efficient transfers, and tighter routing.";
    67	    hotelTier = "4Ōśģ hotel";
    68	    route = "Bangkok + Pattaya";
    69	    nights = "5N / 6D";
    70	  }
    71	
    72	  if (budget.includes("economy")) {
    73	    hotelTier = "3Ōśģ hotel";
    74	  } else if (budget.includes("premium") || budget.includes("luxury")) {
    75	    hotelTier = hotelTier.includes("premium") ? hotelTier : "4Ōśģ premium stay";
    76	  }
    77	
    78	  const notes: string[] = [];
    79	
    80	  if (group.includes("family")) {
    81	    notes.push("family-friendly pacing");
    82	  }
    83	  if (group.includes("friends")) {
    84	    notes.push("group-friendly rooming and transfers");
    85	  }
    86	  if (group.includes("solo")) {
    87	    notes.push("safer central routing");
    88	  }
    89	  if (priority.includes("value")) {
    90	    notes.push("better value balance");
    91	  }
    92	  if (priority.includes("comfort")) {
    93	    notes.push("higher comfort focus");
    94	  }
    95	  if (priority.includes("fast")) {
    96	    notes.push("faster decision-making");
    97	  }
    98	  if (specialRequest) {
    99	    notes.push(`special request noted: ${specialRequest}`);
   100	  }
   101	
   102	  return {
   103	    title,
   104	    summary,
   105	    hotelTier,
   106	    route,
   107	    nights,
   108	    notes,
   109	  };
   110	}
   111	
   112	export function AIGuidedFlow({
   113	  tripStyle = "mixed",
   114	  travellingWith = "couple",
   115	  budget = "comfort",
   116	  priority = "value",
   117	  specialRequest = "",
   118	}: AIGuidedFlowProps) {
   119	  const recommendation = getRecommendation({
   120	    tripStyle,
   121	    travellingWith,
   122	    budget,
   123	    priority,
   124	    specialRequest,
   125	  });
   126	
   127	  return (
   128	    <div className="space-y-4">
   129	      <div className="rounded-3xl border border-slate-200 bg-slate-50 p-5">
   130	        <p className="text-sm font-semibold uppercase tracking-[0.18em] text-sky-600">
   131	          AI recommendation
   132	        </p>
   133	        <h3 className="mt-2 text-2xl font-semibold text-slate-950">
   134	          {recommendation.title}
   135	        </h3>
   136	        <p className="mt-2 text-sm leading-6 text-slate-600">
   137	          {recommendation.summary}
   138	        </p>
   139	      </div>
   140	
   141	      <div className="grid gap-4 md:grid-cols-3">
   142	        <div className="rounded-3xl border border-slate-200 bg-white p-4">
   143	          <p className="text-xs font-semibold uppercase tracking-[0.18em] text-slate-400">
   144	            Route
   145	          </p>
   146	          <p className="mt-2 text-base font-semibold text-slate-950">
   147	            {recommendation.route}
   148	          </p>
   149	        </div>
   150	
   151	        <div className="rounded-3xl border border-slate-200 bg-white p-4">
   152	          <p className="text-xs font-semibold uppercase tracking-[0.18em] text-slate-400">
   153	            Stay style
   154	          </p>
   155	          <p className="mt-2 text-base font-semibold text-slate-950">
   156	            {recommendation.hotelTier}
   157	          </p>
   158	        </div>
   159	
   160	        <div className="rounded-3xl border border-slate-200 bg-white p-4">
   161	          <p className="text-xs font-semibold uppercase tracking-[0.18em] text-slate-400">
   162	            Suggested duration
   163	          </p>
   164	          <p className="mt-2 text-base font-semibold text-slate-950">
   165	            {recommendation.nights}
   166	          </p>
   167	        </div>
   168	      </div>
   169	
   170	      <div className="rounded-3xl border border-slate-200 bg-white p-5">
   171	        <p className="text-sm font-semibold text-slate-950">Why AI picked this</p>
   172	        <div className="mt-3 flex flex-wrap gap-2">
   173	          {recommendation.notes.length > 0 ? (
   174	            recommendation.notes.map((note) => (
   175	              <span
   176	                key={note}
   177	                className="rounded-full border border-slate-200 bg-slate-50 px-3 py-2 text-sm text-slate-700"
   178	              >
   179	                {note}
   180	              </span>
   181	            ))
   182	          ) : (
   183	            <span className="rounded-full border border-slate-200 bg-slate-50 px-3 py-2 text-sm text-slate-700">
   184	              balanced recommendation
   185	            </span>
   186	          )}
   187	        </div>
   188	      </div>
   189	    </div>
   190	  );
   191	}

===== START: src/components/trip-builder/bangkok-area-selector.tsx =====
     1	"use client";
     2	
     3	import { useMemo, useState } from "react";
     4	import { bangkokAreas } from "@/lib/mock/bangkok-builder-data";
     5	import { MapPin, Search } from "lucide-react";
     6	
     7	type Props = {
     8	  value: string;
     9	  onChange: (value: string) => void;
    10	};
    11	
    12	export function BangkokAreaSelector({ value, onChange }: Props) {
    13	  const [query, setQuery] = useState("");
    14	
    15	  const filteredAreas = useMemo(() => {
    16	    const base = bangkokAreas.filter((area) =>
    17	      area.name.toLowerCase().includes(query.toLowerCase())
    18	    );
    19	
    20	    if (query.trim()) return base;
    21	
    22	    const popular = bangkokAreas.filter((area) => area.popular);
    23	    const others = bangkokAreas.filter((area) => !area.popular);
    24	    return [...popular, ...others];
    25	  }, [query]);
    26	
    27	  return (
    28	    <div className="rounded-[28px] border border-slate-200 bg-white p-4 shadow-sm">
    29	      <div className="mb-4 flex items-center gap-2">
    30	        <MapPin className="h-5 w-5 text-sky-600" />
    31	        <div>
    32	          <p className="text-sm font-semibold text-slate-950">
    33	            Where do you want to stay?
    34	          </p>
    35	          <p className="text-xs text-slate-500">
    36	            Choose the city or stay area that should shape better hotel suggestions
    37	          </p>
    38	        </div>
    39	      </div>
    40	
    41	      <div className="relative mb-4">
    42	        <Search className="pointer-events-none absolute left-4 top-1/2 h-4 w-4 -translate-y-1/2 text-slate-400" />
    43	        <input
    44	          type="text"
    45	          placeholder="Search city or area"
    46	          value={query}
    47	          onChange={(e) => setQuery(e.target.value)}
    48	          className="w-full rounded-2xl border border-slate-200 bg-slate-50 py-3 pl-11 pr-4 text-sm text-slate-950 outline-none transition focus:border-sky-400 focus:bg-white"
    49	        />
    50	      </div>
    51	
    52	      <div className="grid gap-3 md:grid-cols-2 xl:grid-cols-3">
    53	        {filteredAreas.map((area) => {
    54	          const active = value === area.name;
    55	
    56	          return (
    57	            <button
    58	              key={area.id}
    59	              type="button"
    60	              onClick={() => onChange(area.name)}
    61	              className={`rounded-2xl border p-4 text-left transition ${
    62	                active
    63	                  ? "border-sky-500 bg-sky-50"
    64	                  : "border-slate-200 bg-slate-50 hover:border-slate-300 hover:bg-white"
    65	              }`}
    66	            >
    67	              <div className="flex items-center justify-between gap-3">
    68	                <span className="text-sm font-semibold text-slate-950">{area.name}</span>
    69	                {area.popular ? (
    70	                  <span className="rounded-full bg-slate-900 px-2.5 py-1 text-[11px] font-medium text-white">
    71	                    Popular
    72	                  </span>
    73	                ) : null}
    74	              </div>
    75	              <p className="mt-2 text-xs leading-5 text-slate-600">{area.shortDescription}</p>
    76	            </button>
    77	          );
    78	        })}
    79	      </div>
    80	    </div>
    81	  );
    82	}===== END: src/components/trip-builder/bangkok-area-selector.tsx =====

    53	                  active ? "bg-sky-500 text-white" : "bg-slate-100 text-slate-700"
    54	                }`}
    55	              >
    56	                <Icon className="h-5 w-5" />

===== START: src/components/trip-builder/city-route-planner.tsx =====
     1	"use client";
     2	
     3	import { useMemo } from "react";
     4	import { MapPin, Plus, Trash2 } from "lucide-react";
     5	import { thailandCities } from "@/lib/mock/bangkok-builder-data";
     6	
     7	export type TripSegment = {
     8	  id: string;
     9	  city: string;
    10	  destinationId?: string;
    11	  checkIn: string;
    12	  checkOut: string;
    13	};
    14	
    15	type Props = {
    16	  segments: TripSegment[];
    17	  onAddSegment: () => void;
    18	  onRemoveSegment: (id: string) => void;
    19	  onUpdateSegment: (
    20	    id: string,
    21	    values: Partial<{
    22	      city: string;
    23	      destinationId?: string;
    24	      checkIn: string;
    25	      checkOut: string;
    26	    }>
    27	  ) => void;
    28	};
    29	
    30	function getNights(checkIn: string, checkOut: string) {
    31	  if (!checkIn || !checkOut) return 0;
    32	
    33	  const start = new Date(checkIn);
    34	  const end = new Date(checkOut);
    35	
    36	  if (Number.isNaN(start.getTime()) || Number.isNaN(end.getTime())) return 0;
    37	
    38	  const diff = Math.floor((end.getTime() - start.getTime()) / (1000 * 60 * 60 * 24));
    39	  return diff > 0 ? diff : 0;
    40	}
    41	
    42	export function CityRoutePlanner({
    43	  segments,
    44	  onAddSegment,
    45	  onRemoveSegment,
    46	  onUpdateSegment,
    47	}: Props) {
    48	  const totalNights = useMemo(
    49	    () => segments.reduce((sum, item) => sum + getNights(item.checkIn, item.checkOut), 0),
    50	    [segments]
    51	  );
    52	
    53	  return (
    54	    <section className="rounded-[32px] border border-slate-200 bg-white p-5 shadow-sm sm:p-6">
    55	      <div className="flex flex-col gap-4 sm:flex-row sm:items-center sm:justify-between">
    56	        <div>
    57	          <div className="flex items-center gap-2">
    58	            <MapPin className="h-5 w-5 text-sky-600" />
    59	            <h2 className="text-lg font-semibold tracking-tight text-slate-950">
    60	              Route planner
    61	            </h2>
    62	          </div>
    63	          <p className="mt-1 text-sm text-slate-600">
    64	            Add one or multiple city stays. Each stop can have its own dates and nights.
    65	          </p>
    66	        </div>
    67	
    68	        <button
    69	          type="button"
    70	          onClick={onAddSegment}
    71	          className="inline-flex items-center justify-center gap-2 rounded-2xl bg-slate-950 px-4 py-3 text-sm font-semibold text-white transition hover:bg-slate-800"
    72	        >
    73	          <Plus className="h-4 w-4" />
    74	          Add city stay
    75	        </button>
    76	      </div>
    77	
    78	      <div className="mt-6 grid gap-4">
    79	        {segments.map((segment, index) => {
    80	          const nights = getNights(segment.checkIn, segment.checkOut);
    81	
    82	          return (
    83	            <div
    84	              key={segment.id}
    85	              className="rounded-[24px] border border-slate-200 bg-slate-50 p-4"
    86	            >
    87	              <div className="mb-4 flex items-center justify-between gap-3">
    88	                <div>
    89	                  <p className="text-sm font-semibold text-slate-950">
    90	                    Stay {index + 1}
    91	                  </p>
    92	                  <p className="text-xs text-slate-500">
    93	                    {nights > 0 ? `${nights} nights selected` : "Select city and dates"}
    94	                  </p>
    95	                </div>
    96	
    97	                {segments.length > 1 ? (
    98	                  <button
    99	                    type="button"
   100	                    onClick={() => onRemoveSegment(segment.id)}
   101	                    className="inline-flex h-10 w-10 items-center justify-center rounded-xl border border-slate-200 bg-white text-slate-600 transition hover:bg-slate-100"
   102	                  >
   103	                    <Trash2 className="h-4 w-4" />
   104	                  </button>
   105	                ) : null}
   106	              </div>
   107	
   108	              <div className="grid gap-4 lg:grid-cols-[1.1fr_0.9fr_0.9fr_0.5fr]">
   109	                <label className="block">
   110	                  <span className="mb-2 block text-sm font-medium text-slate-700">City</span>
   111	                  <select
   112	                    value={segment.city}
   113	                    onChange={(e) => {
   114	                      const selectedCity = thailandCities.find(
   115	                        (city) => city.name === e.target.value
   116	                      );
   117	
   118	                      onUpdateSegment(segment.id, {
   119	                        city: e.target.value,
   120	                        destinationId: selectedCity?.destinationId ?? "",
   121	                      });
   122	                    }}
   123	                    className="w-full rounded-2xl border border-slate-200 bg-white px-4 py-3 text-sm text-slate-950 outline-none transition focus:border-sky-400"
   124	                  >
   125	                    <option value="">Select city</option>
   126	                    {thailandCities.map((city) => (
   127	                      <option key={city.id} value={city.name}>
   128	                        {city.name} ŌĆö {city.region}
   129	                      </option>
   130	                    ))}
   131	                  </select>
   132	                </label>
   133	
   134	                <label className="block">
   135	                  <span className="mb-2 block text-sm font-medium text-slate-700">Check-in</span>
   136	                  <input
   137	                    type="date"
   138	                    value={segment.checkIn}
   139	                    onChange={(e) => onUpdateSegment(segment.id, { checkIn: e.target.value })}
   140	                    className="w-full rounded-2xl border border-slate-200 bg-white px-4 py-3 text-sm text-slate-950 outline-none transition focus:border-sky-400"
   141	                  />
   142	                </label>
   143	
   144	                <label className="block">
   145	                  <span className="mb-2 block text-sm font-medium text-slate-700">Check-out</span>
   146	                  <input
   147	                    type="date"
   148	                    min={segment.checkIn || undefined}
   149	                    value={segment.checkOut}
   150	                    onChange={(e) => onUpdateSegment(segment.id, { checkOut: e.target.value })}
   151	                    className="w-full rounded-2xl border border-slate-200 bg-white px-4 py-3 text-sm text-slate-950 outline-none transition focus:border-sky-400"
   152	                  />
   153	                </label>
   154	
   155	                <div className="block">
   156	                  <span className="mb-2 block text-sm font-medium text-slate-700">Nights</span>
   157	                  <div className="flex h-[50px] items-center rounded-2xl border border-slate-200 bg-white px-4 text-sm font-semibold text-slate-950">
   158	                    {nights || 0}
   159	                  </div>
   160	                </div>
   161	              </div>
   162	            </div>
   163	          );
   164	        })}
   165	      </div>
   166	
   167	      <div className="mt-5 rounded-2xl bg-sky-50 px-4 py-3">
   168	        <p className="text-sm font-medium text-slate-900">
   169	          Total planned trip duration: {totalNights} night{totalNights !== 1 ? "s" : ""}
   170	        </p>
   171	      </div>
   172	    </section>
   173	  );
   174	}===== END: src/components/trip-builder/city-route-planner.tsx =====

===== START: src/components/trip-builder/custom-trip-flow.tsx =====
     1	"use client";
     2	
     3	import { useMemo } from "react";
     4	import { hotels } from "@/data/hotels";
     5	import { transfers } from "@/data/transfers";
     6	import { DateRangePicker } from "./date-range-picker";
     7	import { BangkokAreaSelector } from "./bangkok-area-selector";
     8	import { TravelersSelector } from "./travelers-selector";
     9	import { BudgetSelector } from "./budget-selector";
    10	
    11	type Props = {
    12	  step: number;
    13	  checkIn: string;
    14	  checkOut: string;
    15	  area: string;
    16	  adults: number;
    17	  children: number;
    18	  rooms: number;
    19	  budget: string;
    20	  hotelCategory: string;
    21	  transferType: string;
    22	  selectedSightseeing: string[];
    23	  selectedExtras: string[];
    24	  onDatesChange: (values: { checkIn?: string; checkOut?: string }) => void;
    25	  onAreaChange: (value: string) => void;
    26	  onTravelersChange: (values: { adults?: number; children?: number; rooms?: number }) => void;
    27	  onBudgetChange: (value: string) => void;
    28	  onHotelCategoryChange: (value: string) => void;
    29	  onTransferTypeChange: (value: string) => void;
    30	  onToggleSightseeing: (id: string) => void;
    31	  onToggleExtra: (value: string) => void;
    32	  onStepChange: (step: number) => void;
    33	};

    92	
    93	function normalizeTransferLabel(value: string) {
    94	  if (value === "Premium Private") return "premium-private";
    95	  if (value === "Private") return "private";
    96	  return "shared";
    97	}
    98	
    99	export function CustomTripFlow(props: Props) {
   100	  const activeStep = useMemo(() => Math.min(Math.max(props.step, 1), 6), [props.step]);
   101	
   102	  const matchingHotels = useMemo(
   103	    () =>
   104	      hotels.filter(
   105	        (hotel) =>
   106	          hotel.destinationId === "dest-bangkok" &&
   107	          hotel.category === props.hotelCategory &&
   108	          hotel.isActive
   109	      ),
   110	    [props.hotelCategory]
   111	  );
   112	
   113	  const matchingTransfers = useMemo(() => {
   114	    const type = normalizeTransferLabel(props.transferType);
   115	
   116	    return transfers.filter(
   117	      (item) =>
   118	        item.destinationIds.includes("dest-bangkok") &&
   119	        item.isActive &&
   120	        item.serviceType === type
   121	    );
   122	  }, [props.transferType]);
   123	
   124	  return (
   125	    <div className="space-y-6">
   126	      <div className="rounded-[28px] border border-slate-200 bg-white p-5 shadow-sm">
   127	        <div className="flex flex-wrap gap-2">
   128	          {steps.map((stepLabel, index) => {
   129	            const number = index + 1;
   130	            const active = number === activeStep;
   131	
   132	            return (
   133	              <button
   134	                key={stepLabel}
   135	                type="button"
   136	                onClick={() => props.onStepChange(number)}
   137	                className={`rounded-full px-4 py-2 text-sm font-medium transition ${
   138	                  active
   139	                    ? "bg-slate-950 text-white"
   140	                    : "bg-slate-100 text-slate-700 hover:bg-slate-200"
   141	                }`}
   142	              >
   143	                {number}. {stepLabel}
   144	              </button>
   145	            );
   146	          })}
   147	        </div>
   148	      </div>
   149	
   150	      {activeStep === 1 ? (
   151	        <div className="space-y-6">
   152	          <DateRangePicker
   153	            checkIn={props.checkIn}
   154	            checkOut={props.checkOut}
   155	            onChange={props.onDatesChange}
   156	          />
   157	          <TravelersSelector
   158	            adults={props.adults}
   159	            children={props.children}
   160	            rooms={props.rooms}
   161	            onChange={props.onTravelersChange}
   162	          />
   163	          <BangkokAreaSelector value={props.area} onChange={props.onAreaChange} />
   164	          <BudgetSelector value={props.budget} onChange={props.onBudgetChange} />
   165	        </div>
   166	      ) : null}
   167	
   168	      {activeStep === 2 ? (
   169	        <div className="rounded-[28px] border border-slate-200 bg-white p-5 shadow-sm">
   170	          <p className="text-lg font-semibold tracking-tight text-slate-950">Choose your stay</p>
   171	          <p className="mt-1 text-sm text-slate-600">
   172	            Pick hotel comfort level first. Matching Bangkok hotels are previewed below.
   173	          </p>
   174	
   175	          <div className="mt-5 grid gap-3 md:grid-cols-2 xl:grid-cols-3">
   176	            {hotelCategories.map((item) => {
   177	              const active = props.hotelCategory === item;
   178	              return (
   179	                <button
   180	                  key={item}
   181	                  type="button"
   182	                  onClick={() => props.onHotelCategoryChange(item)}
   183	                  className={`rounded-2xl border p-4 text-left transition ${
   184	                    active
   185	                      ? "border-sky-500 bg-sky-50"
   186	                      : "border-slate-200 bg-slate-50 hover:border-slate-300 hover:bg-white"
   187	                  }`}
   188	                >
   189	                  <p className="text-sm font-semibold text-slate-950">{item}</p>
   190	                </button>
   191	              );
   192	            })}
   193	          </div>
   194	
   195	          <div className="mt-5 grid gap-3 xl:grid-cols-2">
   196	            {matchingHotels.slice(0, 4).map((hotel) => (
   197	              <div
   198	                key={hotel.id}
   199	                className="rounded-2xl border border-slate-200 bg-slate-50 p-4"
   200	              >
   201	                <div className="flex items-start justify-between gap-3">
   202	                  <div>
   203	                    <p className="text-sm font-semibold text-slate-950">{hotel.name}</p>
   204	                    <p className="mt-1 text-xs text-slate-500">
   205	                      {hotel.area} ŌĆó {hotel.category}
   206	                    </p>
   207	                  </div>
   208	                  <span className="rounded-full bg-white px-2.5 py-1 text-[11px] font-medium text-slate-700">
   209	                    {hotel.rating.toFixed(1)}
   210	                  </span>
   211	                </div>
   212	
   213	                <p className="mt-3 text-sm text-slate-600">
   214	                  From Ōé╣{hotel.nightlyRate.toLocaleString("en-IN")} / night
   215	                </p>
   216	              </div>
   217	            ))}
   218	          </div>
   219	        </div>
   220	      ) : null}
   221	
   222	      {activeStep === 3 ? (
   223	        <div className="rounded-[28px] border border-slate-200 bg-white p-5 shadow-sm">
   224	          <p className="text-lg font-semibold tracking-tight text-slate-950">Choose transfers</p>
   225	          <p className="mt-1 text-sm text-slate-600">
   226	            This controls the movement style. Vehicle size is auto-handled later from passenger count.
   227	          </p>
   228	
   229	          <div className="mt-5 grid gap-3 md:grid-cols-3">
   230	            {transferOptions.map((item) => {
   231	              const active = props.transferType === item;
   232	              return (
   233	                <button
   234	                  key={item}
   235	                  type="button"
   236	                  onClick={() => props.onTransferTypeChange(item)}
   237	                  className={`rounded-2xl border p-4 text-left transition ${
   238	                    active
   239	                      ? "border-sky-500 bg-sky-50"
   240	                      : "border-slate-200 bg-slate-50 hover:border-slate-300 hover:bg-white"
   241	                  }`}
   242	                >
   243	                  <p className="text-sm font-semibold text-slate-950">{item}</p>
   244	                </button>
   245	              );
   246	            })}
   247	          </div>
   248	
   249	          <div className="mt-5 grid gap-3 xl:grid-cols-2">
   250	            {matchingTransfers.slice(0, 4).map((item) => (
   251	              <div
   252	                key={item.id}
   253	                className="rounded-2xl border border-slate-200 bg-slate-50 p-4"
   254	              >
   255	                <p className="text-sm font-semibold text-slate-950">{item.name}</p>
   256	                <p className="mt-1 text-xs text-slate-500">
   257	                  {item.vehicleClass} ŌĆó {item.purpose}
   258	                </p>
   259	                <p className="mt-3 text-sm text-slate-600">
   260	                  Ōé╣{item.price.toLocaleString("en-IN")}
   261	                </p>
   262	              </div>
   263	            ))}
   264	          </div>
   265	        </div>
   266	      ) : null}
   267	
   268	      {activeStep === 4 ? (
   269	        <div className="rounded-[28px] border border-slate-200 bg-white p-5 shadow-sm">
   270	          <p className="text-lg font-semibold tracking-tight text-slate-950">Add sightseeing</p>
   271	          <p className="mt-1 text-sm text-slate-600">
   272	            Choose activities that fit your trip rhythm. These are placeholder Bangkok options for now.
   273	          </p>
   274	
   275	          <div className="mt-5 grid gap-4 xl:grid-cols-2">
   276	            {sightseeingItems.map((item) => {
   277	              const active = props.selectedSightseeing.includes(item.id);
   278	              return (
   279	                <button
   280	                  key={item.id}
   281	                  type="button"
   282	                  onClick={() => props.onToggleSightseeing(item.id)}
   283	                  className={`rounded-[24px] border p-4 text-left transition ${
   284	                    active
   285	                      ? "border-sky-500 bg-sky-50"
   286	                      : "border-slate-200 bg-slate-50 hover:border-slate-300 hover:bg-white"
   287	                  }`}
   288	                >
   289	                  <div className="flex items-start justify-between gap-4">
   290	                    <div>
   291	                      <span className="rounded-full bg-white px-2.5 py-1 text-[11px] font-medium text-slate-700">
   292	                        {item.category}
   293	                      </span>
   294	                      <p className="mt-3 text-base font-semibold text-slate-950">
   295	                        {item.title}
   296	                      </p>
   297	                      <p className="mt-1 text-sm text-slate-600">{item.duration}</p>
   298	                    </div>
   299	
   300	                    <p className="text-sm font-semibold text-slate-950">
   301	                      Ōé╣{item.price.toLocaleString("en-IN")}
   302	                    </p>
   303	                  </div>
   304	                </button>
   305	              );
   306	            })}
   307	          </div>
   308	        </div>
   309	      ) : null}
   310	
   311	      {activeStep === 5 ? (
   312	        <div className="rounded-[28px] border border-slate-200 bg-white p-5 shadow-sm">
   313	          <p className="text-lg font-semibold tracking-tight text-slate-950">Add useful extras</p>
   314	          <p className="mt-1 text-sm text-slate-600">Choose the extras you want included.</p>
   315	
   316	          <div className="mt-5 flex flex-wrap gap-3">
   317	            {extraOptions.map((item) => {
   318	              const active = props.selectedExtras.includes(item);
   319	              return (
   320	                <button
   321	                  key={item}
   322	                  type="button"
   323	                  onClick={() => props.onToggleExtra(item)}
   324	                  className={`rounded-full px-4 py-2 text-sm font-medium transition ${
   325	                    active
   326	                      ? "bg-sky-500 text-white"
   327	                      : "bg-slate-100 text-slate-700 hover:bg-slate-200"
   328	                  }`}
   329	                >
   330	                  {item}
   331	                </button>
   332	              );
   333	            })}
   334	          </div>
   335	        </div>
   336	      ) : null}
   337	
   338	      {activeStep === 6 ? (
   339	        <div className="rounded-[28px] border border-slate-200 bg-white p-5 shadow-sm">
   340	          <p className="text-lg font-semibold tracking-tight text-slate-950">
   341	            Review your custom trip
   342	          </p>
   343	          <div className="mt-5 grid gap-3 md:grid-cols-2">
   344	            <ReviewCard label="Area" value={props.area || "Not selected"} />
   345	            <ReviewCard label="Budget" value={props.budget || "Not selected"} />
   346	            <ReviewCard label="Hotel category" value={props.hotelCategory || "Not selected"} />
   347	            <ReviewCard label="Transfers" value={props.transferType || "Not selected"} />
   348	            <ReviewCard
   349	              label="Sightseeing"
   350	              value={`${props.selectedSightseeing.length} selected`}
   351	            />
   352	            <ReviewCard label="Extras" value={`${props.selectedExtras.length} selected`} />
   353	          </div>
   354	        </div>
   355	      ) : null}
   356	
   357	      <div className="flex items-center justify-between gap-3">
   358	        <button
   359	          type="button"
   360	          onClick={() => props.onStepChange(Math.max(1, activeStep - 1))}
   361	          className="rounded-2xl border border-slate-200 bg-white px-5 py-3 text-sm font-semibold text-slate-800 transition hover:bg-slate-50"
   362	        >
   363	          Back
   364	        </button>
   365	
   366	        <button
   367	          type="button"
   368	          onClick={() => props.onStepChange(Math.min(6, activeStep + 1))}
   369	          className="rounded-2xl bg-slate-950 px-5 py-3 text-sm font-semibold text-white transition hover:bg-slate-800"
   370	        >
   371	          {activeStep === 6 ? "Continue booking" : "Next step"}
   372	        </button>
   373	      </div>
   374	    </div>
   375	  );
   376	}
   377	
   378	function ReviewCard({ label, value }: { label: string; value: string }) {

   382	      <p className="mt-2 text-sm font-semibold text-slate-950">{value}</p>
   383	    </div>
   384	  );

===== START: src/components/trip-builder/date-range-picker.tsx =====
     1	"use client";
     2	
     3	import { useMemo } from "react";
     4	import { CalendarDays } from "lucide-react";
     5	
     6	type Props = {
     7	  checkIn: string;
     8	  checkOut: string;
     9	  onChange: (values: { checkIn?: string; checkOut?: string }) => void;
    10	};
    11	
    12	function getNights(checkIn: string, checkOut: string) {
    13	  if (!checkIn || !checkOut) return 0;
    14	
    15	  const start = new Date(checkIn);
    16	  const end = new Date(checkOut);
    17	
    18	  if (Number.isNaN(start.getTime()) || Number.isNaN(end.getTime())) return 0;
    19	
    20	  const diffMs = end.getTime() - start.getTime();
    21	  const diffDays = Math.floor(diffMs / (1000 * 60 * 60 * 24));
    22	
    23	  return diffDays > 0 ? diffDays : 0;
    24	}
    25	
    26	function formatDateLabel(value: string) {
    27	  if (!value) return "";
    28	
    29	  const date = new Date(value);
    30	  if (Number.isNaN(date.getTime())) return value;
    31	
    32	  return date.toLocaleDateString("en-GB", {
    33	    day: "2-digit",
    34	    month: "short",
    35	  });
    36	}
    37	
    38	function getTodayDateString() {
    39	  const today = new Date();
    40	  const year = today.getFullYear();
    41	  const month = `${today.getMonth() + 1}`.padStart(2, "0");
    42	  const day = `${today.getDate()}`.padStart(2, "0");
    43	  return `${year}-${month}-${day}`;
    44	}
    45	
    46	export function DateRangePicker({ checkIn, checkOut, onChange }: Props) {
    47	  const nights = useMemo(() => getNights(checkIn, checkOut), [checkIn, checkOut]);
    48	  const today = useMemo(() => getTodayDateString(), []);
    49	
    50	  const summary = useMemo(() => {
    51	    if (!checkIn || !checkOut || nights <= 0) {
    52	      return "Select check-in and check-out";
    53	    }
    54	
    55	    return `${formatDateLabel(checkIn)} ŌåÆ ${formatDateLabel(checkOut)} ┬Ę ${nights} Night${
    56	      nights > 1 ? "s" : ""
    57	    }`;
    58	  }, [checkIn, checkOut, nights]);
    59	
    60	  return (
    61	    <div className="rounded-[28px] border border-slate-200 bg-white p-4 shadow-sm">
    62	      <div className="mb-4 flex items-center gap-2">
    63	        <CalendarDays className="h-5 w-5 text-sky-600" />
    64	        <div>
    65	          <p className="text-sm font-semibold text-slate-950">Travel dates</p>
    66	          <p className="text-xs text-slate-500">Trip duration is calculated automatically</p>
    67	        </div>
    68	      </div>
    69	
    70	      <div className="grid gap-4 md:grid-cols-2">
    71	        <label className="block">
    72	          <span className="mb-2 block text-sm font-medium text-slate-700">Check-in</span>
    73	          <input
    74	            type="date"
    75	            min={today}
    76	            value={checkIn}
    77	            onChange={(e) => onChange({ checkIn: e.target.value })}
    78	            className="w-full rounded-2xl border border-slate-200 bg-slate-50 px-4 py-3 text-sm text-slate-950 outline-none transition focus:border-sky-400 focus:bg-white"
    79	          />
    80	        </label>
    81	
    82	        <label className="block">
    83	          <span className="mb-2 block text-sm font-medium text-slate-700">Check-out</span>
    84	          <input
    85	            type="date"
    86	            value={checkOut}
    87	            min={checkIn || today}
    88	            onChange={(e) => onChange({ checkOut: e.target.value })}
    89	            className="w-full rounded-2xl border border-slate-200 bg-slate-50 px-4 py-3 text-sm text-slate-950 outline-none transition focus:border-sky-400 focus:bg-white"
    90	          />
    91	        </label>
    92	      </div>
    93	
    94	      <div className="mt-4 rounded-2xl bg-slate-50 px-4 py-3">
    95	        <p className="text-sm font-medium text-slate-800">{summary}</p>
    96	        <p className="mt-1 text-xs text-slate-500">
    97	          {nights > 0 ? `${nights} Nights ┬Ę ${nights + 1} Days` : "Trip duration will appear here"}
    98	        </p>
    99	      </div>
   100	    </div>
   101	  );
   102	}===== END: src/components/trip-builder/date-range-picker.tsx =====
