     1	"use client";
     2	
     3	type Props = {
     4	  adults: number;
     5	  children: number;
     6	  rooms: number;
     7	  onChange: (values: { adults?: number; children?: number; rooms?: number }) => void;
     8	};
     9	
    10	function Counter({
    11	  label,
    12	  value,
    13	  min = 0,
    14	  onChange,
    15	}: {
    16	  label: string;
    17	  value: number;
    18	  min?: number;
    19	  onChange: (next: number) => void;
    20	}) {
    21	  return (
    22	    <div className="rounded-2xl border border-slate-200 bg-slate-50 p-4">
    23	      <div className="flex items-center justify-between gap-3">
    24	        <span className="text-sm font-medium text-slate-800">{label}</span>
    25	        <div className="flex items-center gap-2">
    26	          <button
    27	            type="button"
    28	            onClick={() => onChange(Math.max(min, value - 1))}
    29	            className="h-9 w-9 rounded-xl border border-slate-200 bg-white text-slate-800"
    30	          >
    31	            -
    32	          </button>
    33	          <span className="w-8 text-center text-sm font-semibold text-slate-950">{value}</span>
    34	          <button
    35	            type="button"
    36	            onClick={() => onChange(value + 1)}
    37	            className="h-9 w-9 rounded-xl border border-slate-200 bg-white text-slate-800"
    38	          >
    39	            +
    40	          </button>
    41	        </div>
    42	      </div>
    43	    </div>
    44	  );
    45	}
    46	
    47	export function TravelersSelector({ adults, children, rooms, onChange }: Props) {
    48	  return (
    49	    <div className="rounded-[28px] border border-slate-200 bg-white p-4 shadow-sm">
    50	      <div className="mb-4">
    51	        <p className="text-sm font-semibold text-slate-950">Who is travelling?</p>
    52	        <p className="text-xs text-slate-500">Set travellers and rooms</p>
    53	      </div>
    54	
    55	      <div className="grid gap-3 md:grid-cols-3">
    56	        <Counter label="Adults" value={adults} min={1} onChange={(next) => onChange({ adults: next })} />
    57	        <Counter label="Children" value={children} min={0} onChange={(next) => onChange({ children: next })} />
    58	        <Counter label="Rooms" value={rooms} min={1} onChange={(next) => onChange({ rooms: next })} />
    59	      </div>
    60	    </div>
    61	  );
    62	}===== END: src/components/trip-builder/travelers-selector.tsx =====

   441	
   442	function formatINR(value: number) {
   443	  return new Intl.NumberFormat("en-IN", {
   444	    style: "currency",
   445	    currency: "INR",
   446	    maximumFractionDigits: 0,
   447	  }).format(value);
   448	}
   449	
   450	function getTomorrowISODate() {
   451	  const date = new Date();
   452	  date.setDate(date.getDate() + 1);
   453	  return date.toISOString().slice(0, 10);
   454	}
   455	
   456	function formatLongDate(value: string) {
   457	  if (!value) return "Not selected";
   458	  const date = new Date(value);
   459	  if (Number.isNaN(date.getTime())) return value;
   460	
   461	  return new Intl.DateTimeFormat("en-GB", {
   462	    day: "2-digit",
   463	    month: "short",
   464	    year: "numeric",
   465	  }).format(date);
   466	}
   467	
   468	function clampMinimum(value: number, min: number) {
   469	  return Math.max(min, value);
   470	}
   471	
   472	function getTotalTravellers(adults: number, children: number) {
   473	  return adults + children;
   474	}
   475	
   476	function calculatePackagePrice(
   477	  pkg: StandardPackage,
   478	  adults: number,
   479	  children: number,
   480	  rooms: number,
   481	) {
   482	  const adultTotal = pkg.basePricePerPerson * adults;
   483	  const childTotal = Math.round(pkg.basePricePerPerson * 0.72 * children);
   484	  const roomAdjustment = Math.max(0, rooms - 1) * 3500;
   485	  const serviceFee = Math.round((adultTotal + childTotal + roomAdjustment) * 0.05);
   486	
   487	  const total = adultTotal + childTotal + roomAdjustment + serviceFee;
   488	
   489	  return {
   490	    pricePerPerson: pkg.basePricePerPerson,
   491	    totalPrice: Math.round(total),
   492	  };
   493	}
   494	
   495	export function TripBuilderShell() {
   496	  const [mode, setMode] = useState<BuilderMode>("standard");
   497	  const [activeCategory, setActiveCategory] = useState<PackageCategory>("all");
   498	
   499	  const [departureCity, setDepartureCity] = useState("Bangalore");
   500	  const [destinationCity, setDestinationCity] = useState("Bangkok");
   501	  const [departureDate, setDepartureDate] = useState(getTomorrowISODate());
   502	
   503	  const [adults, setAdults] = useState(2);
   504	  const [children, setChildren] = useState(0);
   505	  const [rooms, setRooms] = useState(1);
   506	
   507	  const [selectedPackageId, setSelectedPackageId] = useState<string | null>(null);
   508	  const [detailPackageId, setDetailPackageId] = useState<string | null>(null);
   509	  const [customSeedPackageId, setCustomSeedPackageId] = useState<string | null>(null);
   510	
   511	  const totalTravellers = getTotalTravellers(adults, children);
   512	
   513	  const filteredPackages = useMemo(() => {
   514	    return standardPackages.filter((pkg) =>
   515	      activeCategory === "all" ? true : pkg.category.includes(activeCategory),
   516	    );
   517	  }, [activeCategory]);
   518	
   519	  const packageCards = useMemo(() => {
   520	    return filteredPackages.map((pkg) => ({
   521	      ...pkg,
   522	      pricing: calculatePackagePrice(pkg, adults, children, rooms),
   523	    }));
   524	  }, [filteredPackages, adults, children, rooms]);
   525	
   526	  const selectedPackage =
   527	    packageCards.find((pkg) => pkg.id === selectedPackageId) ?? null;
   528	
   529	  const detailPackage =
   530	    packageCards.find((pkg) => pkg.id === detailPackageId) ?? null;
   531	
   532	  function handleSelectPackage(packageId: string) {
   533	    setSelectedPackageId(packageId);
   534	  }
   535	
   536	  function handleOpenDetail(packageId: string) {
   537	    setDetailPackageId(packageId);
   538	  }
   539	
   540	  function handleCloseDetail() {
   541	    setDetailPackageId(null);
   542	  }
   543	
   544	  function handleCustomizePackage(packageId: string) {
   545	    setSelectedPackageId(packageId);
   546	    setCustomSeedPackageId(packageId);
   547	    setMode("custom");
   548	    setDetailPackageId(null);
   549	  }
   550	
   551	  return (
   552	    <div className="min-h-screen bg-slate-50">
   553	      <header className="sticky top-0 z-40 border-b border-slate-200 bg-white/95 backdrop-blur">
   554	        <div className="mx-auto flex max-w-7xl items-center justify-between px-4 py-4 sm:px-6 lg:px-8">
   555	          <Link href="/" className="flex items-center gap-3">
   556	            <div className="rounded-full bg-sky-100 px-3 py-1 text-[11px] font-semibold uppercase tracking-[0.22em] text-sky-700">
   557	              EasyTrip365
   558	            </div>
   559	            <div className="hidden text-sm font-medium text-slate-600 md:block">
   560	              Thailand Planner
   561	            </div>
   562	          </Link>
   563	
   564	          <nav className="hidden items-center gap-6 md:flex">
   565	            <Link href="/" className="text-sm font-medium text-slate-600 hover:text-slate-950">
   566	              Home
   567	            </Link>
   568	            <Link href="/results" className="text-sm font-medium text-slate-600 hover:text-slate-950">
   569	              Packages
   570	            </Link>
   571	            <Link href="/customize" className="text-sm font-medium text-slate-600 hover:text-slate-950">
   572	              Custom
   573	            </Link>
   574	            <Link href="/review" className="text-sm font-medium text-slate-600 hover:text-slate-950">
   575	              Review
   576	            </Link>
   577	          </nav>
   578	
   579	          <button
   580	            type="button"
   581	            className="inline-flex h-10 w-10 items-center justify-center rounded-full border border-slate-200 bg-white text-slate-700 md:hidden"
   582	            aria-label="Open menu"
   583	          >
   584	            <Menu className="h-5 w-5" />
   585	          </button>
   586	        </div>
   587	      </header>
   588	
   589	      <section className="border-b border-slate-200 bg-[linear-gradient(180deg,#0a2a52_0%,#0d305f_100%)]">
   590	        <div className="mx-auto max-w-7xl px-4 py-5 sm:px-6 lg:px-8">
   591	          <div className="grid gap-3 lg:grid-cols-[1.1fr_1.1fr_1fr_1fr_180px]">
   592	            <SearchField
   593	              label="Starting From"
   594	              value={departureCity}
   595	              onChange={setDepartureCity}
   596	              icon={<MapPin className="h-4 w-4" />}
   597	            />
   598	            <SearchField
   599	              label="Going To"
   600	              value={destinationCity}
   601	              onChange={setDestinationCity}
   602	              icon={<MapPin className="h-4 w-4" />}
   603	            />
   604	            <SearchField
   605	              label="Departure Date"
   606	              value={departureDate}
   607	              onChange={setDepartureDate}
   608	              type="date"
   609	              min={getTomorrowISODate()}
   610	              icon={<CalendarDays className="h-4 w-4" />}
   611	            />
   612	            <GuestsField
   613	              adults={adults}
   614	              children={children}
   615	              rooms={rooms}
   616	              setAdults={setAdults}
   617	              setChildren={setChildren}
   618	              setRooms={setRooms}
   619	            />
   620	            <button
   621	              type="button"
   622	              className="inline-flex items-center justify-center rounded-2xl bg-sky-500 px-4 py-4 text-sm font-semibold text-white transition hover:bg-sky-600"
   623	            >
   624	              Search
   625	            </button>
   626	          </div>
   627	        </div>
   628	      </section>
   629	
   630	      <main className="mx-auto max-w-7xl px-4 py-6 sm:px-6 lg:px-8">
   631	        <div className="grid gap-4 md:grid-cols-3">
   632	          <ModeCard
   633	            active={mode === "standard"}
   634	            title="Standard Packages"
   635	            description="Curated itineraries with fixed routing and cleaner comparisons."
   636	            onClick={() => setMode("standard")}
   637	            icon={<MapPin className="h-5 w-5" />}
   638	          />
   639	          <ModeCard
   640	            active={mode === "ai"}
   641	            title="AI Guided"
   642	            description="Use AI when the customer wants help choosing a route."
   643	            onClick={() => setMode("ai")}
   644	            icon={<Sparkles className="h-5 w-5" />}
   645	          />
   646	          <ModeCard
   647	            active={mode === "custom"}
   648	            title="Custom Trip"
   649	            description="Build city-night splits like 2N Bangkok ┬Ę 2N Krabi ┬Ę 2N Pattaya."
   650	            onClick={() => setMode("custom")}
   651	            icon={<ChevronRight className="h-5 w-5" />}
   652	          />
   653	        </div>
   654	
   655	        {mode === "standard" && (
   656	          <div className="mt-6 space-y-6">
   657	            <section className="overflow-hidden rounded-[30px] border border-slate-200 bg-white shadow-sm">
   658	              <div className="border-b border-slate-200 px-4 py-4 sm:px-6">
   659	                <div className="flex flex-wrap items-center gap-4">
   660	                  {categoryTabs.map((tab) => {
   661	                    const active = activeCategory === tab.value;
   662	
   663	                    return (
   664	                      <button
   665	                        key={tab.value}
   666	                        type="button"
   667	                        onClick={() => setActiveCategory(tab.value)}
   668	                        className={`relative pb-3 text-sm font-semibold transition ${
   669	                          active ? "text-sky-600" : "text-slate-500 hover:text-slate-900"
   670	                        }`}
   671	                      >
   672	                        {tab.label}
   673	                        {active ? (
   674	                          <span className="absolute inset-x-0 bottom-0 h-0.5 rounded-full bg-sky-500" />
   675	                        ) : null}
   676	                      </button>
   677	                    );
   678	                  })}
   679	                </div>
   680	              </div>
   681	
   682	              <div className="grid gap-6 p-4 sm:p-6 xl:grid-cols-[minmax(0,1fr)_340px]">
   683	                <div className="space-y-5">
   684	                  <div className="rounded-3xl border border-slate-200 bg-slate-50 px-4 py-4">
   685	                    <p className="text-sm font-semibold text-slate-900">
   686	                      Recommended Standard Packages
   687	                    </p>
   688	                    <p className="mt-1 text-sm text-slate-500">
   689	                      Showing curated Thailand packages for{" "}
   690	                      <span className="font-semibold text-slate-900">
   691	                        {departureCity}
   692	                      </span>{" "}
   693	                      departing on{" "}
   694	                      <span className="font-semibold text-slate-900">
   695	                        {formatLongDate(departureDate)}
   696	                      </span>
   697	                      .
   698	                    </p>
   699	                  </div>
   700	
   701	                  <div className="grid gap-5 lg:grid-cols-2">
   702	                    {packageCards.map((pkg) => (
   703	                      <article
   704	                        key={pkg.id}
   705	                        className="overflow-hidden rounded-[28px] border border-slate-200 bg-white shadow-sm"
   706	                      >
   707	                        <div
   708	                          className={`h-52 bg-gradient-to-br ${pkg.accentFrom} ${pkg.accentTo} relative`}
   709	                        >
   710	                          <div className="absolute left-4 top-4 rounded-full bg-white/90 px-3 py-1 text-xs font-semibold text-slate-900">
   711	                            {pkg.badge}
   712	                          </div>
   713	                          <div className="absolute bottom-4 left-4 right-4 rounded-2xl bg-white/90 p-3 backdrop-blur">
   714	                            <p className="text-base font-semibold text-slate-950">
   715	                              {pkg.title}
   716	                            </p>
   717	                            <p className="mt-1 text-sm text-slate-600">
   718	                              {pkg.citySplit
   719	                                .map((item) => `${item.nights}N ${item.city}`)
   720	                                .join(" ┬Ę ")}
   721	                            </p>
   722	                          </div>
   723	                        </div>
   724	
   725	                        <div className="p-5">
   726	                          <p className="text-sm text-slate-600">{pkg.subtitle}</p>
   727	
   728	                          <div className="mt-4 grid grid-cols-2 gap-3 text-sm">
   729	                            <FactPill label={`${pkg.durationNights}N / ${pkg.durationDays}D`} />
   730	                            <FactPill label={pkg.hotelCategory} />
   731	                            <FactPill label={pkg.includedFlights ? "With flights" : "Without flights"} />
   732	                            <FactPill label={`${pkg.activitiesCount} activities`} />
   733	                          </div>
   734	
   735	                          <div className="mt-4 grid gap-2 text-sm text-slate-700 sm:grid-cols-2">
   736	                            <InfoBullet text={pkg.transferType} />
   737	                            <InfoBullet text={pkg.mealsLabel} />
   738	                            {pkg.highlightList.slice(0, 4).map((item) => (
   739	                              <InfoBullet key={item} text={item} />
   740	                            ))}
   741	                          </div>
   742	
   743	                          <div className="mt-4 flex flex-wrap gap-2">
   744	                            {pkg.bestFor.map((item) => (
   745	                              <span
   746	                                key={item}
   747	                                className="rounded-full border border-slate-200 bg-slate-50 px-3 py-1.5 text-xs font-medium text-slate-600"
   748	                              >
   749	                                {item}
   750	                              </span>
   751	                            ))}
   752	                          </div>
   753	
   754	                          <div className="mt-5 rounded-2xl bg-slate-50 p-4">
   755	                            <div className="flex items-end justify-between gap-4">
   756	                              <div>
   757	                                <p className="text-sm text-slate-500">From</p>
   758	                                <p className="text-2xl font-semibold text-slate-950">
   759	                                  {formatINR(pkg.pricing.pricePerPerson)}
   760	                                  <span className="ml-1 text-sm font-medium text-slate-500">
   761	                                    / person
   762	                                  </span>
   763	                                </p>
   764	                              </div>
   765	                              <div className="text-right">
   766	                                <p className="text-sm text-slate-500">Total</p>
   767	                                <p className="text-lg font-semibold text-slate-950">
   768	                                  {formatINR(pkg.pricing.totalPrice)}
   769	                                </p>
   770	                              </div>
   771	                            </div>
   772	                          </div>
   773	
   774	                          <div className="mt-5 grid gap-2 sm:grid-cols-2">
   775	                            <button
   776	                              type="button"
   777	                              onClick={() => handleOpenDetail(pkg.id)}
   778	                              className="rounded-full border border-slate-200 bg-white px-4 py-3 text-sm font-semibold text-slate-700 transition hover:border-slate-300"
   779	                            >
   780	                              View itinerary
   781	                            </button>
   782	                            <button
   783	                              type="button"
   784	                              onClick={() => handleSelectPackage(pkg.id)}
   785	                              className="rounded-full bg-slate-950 px-4 py-3 text-sm font-semibold text-white transition hover:bg-slate-800"
   786	                            >
   787	                              Choose package
   788	                            </button>
   789	                          </div>
   790	
   791	                          <button
   792	                            type="button"
   793	                            onClick={() => handleCustomizePackage(pkg.id)}
   794	                            className="mt-2 w-full rounded-full border border-sky-200 bg-sky-50 px-4 py-3 text-sm font-semibold text-sky-700 transition hover:bg-sky-100"
   795	                          >
   796	                            Customize this package
   797	                          </button>
   798	                        </div>
   799	                      </article>
   800	                    ))}
   801	                  </div>
   802	                </div>
   803	
   804	                <aside className="space-y-4">
   805	                  <div className="rounded-[28px] border border-slate-200 bg-white p-5 shadow-sm">
   806	                    <p className="text-sm font-semibold uppercase tracking-[0.18em] text-sky-600">
   807	                      Trip Summary
   808	                    </p>
   809	                    <div className="mt-4 space-y-3">
   810	                      <SummaryRow label="From" value={departureCity} />
   811	                      <SummaryRow label="Destination" value={destinationCity} />
   812	                      <SummaryRow label="Departure" value={formatLongDate(departureDate)} />
   813	                      <SummaryRow
   814	                        label="Guests"
   815	                        value={`${adults} Adults${children ? `, ${children} Children` : ""}`}
   816	                      />
   817	                      <SummaryRow label="Rooms" value={`${rooms}`} />
   818	                    </div>
   819	
   820	                    {selectedPackage ? (
   821	                      <div className="mt-4 rounded-2xl bg-sky-50 p-4">
   822	                        <p className="text-xs font-semibold uppercase tracking-[0.18em] text-sky-600">
   823	                          Selected package
   824	                        </p>
   825	                        <p className="mt-2 text-lg font-semibold text-slate-950">
   826	                          {selectedPackage.title}
   827	                        </p>
   828	                        <p className="mt-1 text-sm text-slate-600">
   829	                          {selectedPackage.citySplit
   830	                            .map((item) => `${item.nights}N ${item.city}`)
   831	                            .join(" ┬Ę ")}
   832	                        </p>
   833	                        <p className="mt-3 text-2xl font-semibold text-slate-950">
   834	                          {formatINR(selectedPackage.pricing.totalPrice)}
   835	                        </p>
   836	                      </div>
   837	                    ) : (
   838	                      <div className="mt-4 rounded-2xl border border-dashed border-slate-300 bg-slate-50 p-4 text-sm text-slate-500">
   839	                        No package selected yet.
   840	                      </div>
   841	                    )}
   842	
   843	                    <button
   844	                      type="button"
   845	                      disabled={!selectedPackage}
   846	                      className={`mt-5 w-full rounded-full px-4 py-3 text-sm font-semibold transition ${
   847	                        selectedPackage
   848	                          ? "bg-slate-950 text-white hover:bg-slate-800"
   849	                          : "cursor-not-allowed bg-slate-200 text-slate-500"
   850	                      }`}
   851	                    >
   852	                      Continue booking
   853	                    </button>
   854	                  </div>
   855	
   856	                  <div className="rounded-[28px] border border-sky-200 bg-gradient-to-br from-sky-50 to-cyan-50 p-5">
   857	                    <p className="text-sm font-semibold text-sky-700">
   858	                      Need a different city split?
   859	                    </p>
   860	                    <p className="mt-2 text-sm leading-6 text-slate-600">
   861	                      Standard packages keep the route fixed. The moment a customer
   862	                      wants to change nights, cities, hotels, transfers, or activities,
   863	                      move them into Custom.
   864	                    </p>
   865	                  </div>
   866	                </aside>
   867	              </div>
   868	            </section>
   869	          </div>
   870	        )}
   871	
   872	        {mode === "ai" && (
   873	          <section className="mt-6 rounded-[30px] border border-slate-200 bg-white p-6 shadow-sm">
   874	            <AIGuidedFlow />
   875	          </section>
   876	        )}
   877	
   878	        {mode === "custom" && (
   879	          <section className="mt-6 rounded-[30px] border border-slate-200 bg-white p-6 shadow-sm">
   880	            <div className="mb-4 rounded-3xl border border-sky-200 bg-sky-50 p-4">
   881	              <p className="text-sm font-semibold text-sky-700">Custom mode enabled</p>
   882	              <p className="mt-1 text-sm text-slate-600">
   883	                Build city-night splits like 2N Bangkok ┬Ę 2N Krabi ┬Ę 2N Pattaya and
   884	                edit day-level items freely.
   885	              </p>
   886	              {customSeedPackageId ? (
   887	                <p className="mt-2 text-sm text-slate-700">
   888	                  Starting from package:{" "}
   889	                  <span className="font-semibold">
   890	                    {standardPackages.find((pkg) => pkg.id === customSeedPackageId)?.title ??
   891	                      "Selected package"}
   892	                  </span>
   893	                </p>
   894	              ) : null}
   895	            </div>
   896	
   897	            <CustomTripFlow />
   898	          </section>
   899	        )}
   900	      </main>
   901	
   902	      {detailPackage ? (
   903	        <div className="fixed inset-0 z-50 bg-slate-950/50 p-4 backdrop-blur-sm">
   904	          <div className="mx-auto flex h-full max-w-5xl flex-col overflow-hidden rounded-[30px] bg-white shadow-2xl">
   905	            <div className="flex items-start justify-between border-b border-slate-200 px-6 py-5">
   906	              <div>
   907	                <p className="text-sm font-semibold uppercase tracking-[0.18em] text-sky-600">
   908	                  Standard Package Detail
   909	                </p>
   910	                <h2 className="mt-2 text-2xl font-semibold text-slate-950">
   911	                  {detailPackage.title}
   912	                </h2>
   913	                <p className="mt-1 text-sm text-slate-600">
   914	                  {detailPackage.citySplit
   915	                    .map((item) => `${item.nights}N ${item.city}`)
   916	                    .join(" ┬Ę ")}
   917	                </p>
   918	              </div>
   919	              <button
   920	                type="button"
   921	                onClick={handleCloseDetail}
   922	                className="inline-flex h-10 w-10 items-center justify-center rounded-full border border-slate-200 text-slate-600"
   923	              >
   924	                <X className="h-5 w-5" />
   925	              </button>
   926	            </div>
   927	
   928	            <div className="grid min-h-0 flex-1 gap-0 lg:grid-cols-[minmax(0,1fr)_320px]">
   929	              <div className="overflow-y-auto px-6 py-5">
   930	                <div className={`rounded-[26px] bg-gradient-to-br ${detailPackage.accentFrom} ${detailPackage.accentTo} p-6`}>
   931	                  <p className="text-sm font-semibold text-slate-700">
   932	                    {detailPackage.subtitle}
   933	                  </p>
   934	                  <div className="mt-4 flex flex-wrap gap-2">
   935	                    {detailPackage.citySplit.map((item) => (
   936	                      <span
   937	                        key={`${detailPackage.id}-${item.city}`}
   938	                        className="rounded-full bg-white/85 px-4 py-2 text-sm font-semibold text-slate-900"
   939	                      >
   940	                        {item.nights}N {item.city}
   941	                      </span>
   942	                    ))}
   943	                  </div>
   944	                </div>
   945	
   946	                <div className="mt-6 grid gap-4 sm:grid-cols-3">
   947	                  <DetailInfoCard label="Hotel" value={detailPackage.hotelCategory} />
   948	                  <DetailInfoCard label="Transfers" value={detailPackage.transferType} />
   949	                  <DetailInfoCard
   950	                    label="Meals"
   951	                    value={detailPackage.mealsLabel}
   952	                  />
   953	                </div>
   954	
   955	                <div className="mt-6">
   956	                  <p className="text-lg font-semibold text-slate-950">Day-wise itinerary</p>
   957	                  <p className="mt-1 text-sm text-slate-500">
   958	                    This is the standard plan. Editing any day should move the trip into Custom.
   959	                  </p>
   960	
   961	                  <div className="mt-5 space-y-4">
   962	                    {detailPackage.dayPlan.map((item) => (
   963	                      <div
   964	                        key={`${detailPackage.id}-day-${item.day}`}
   965	                        className="rounded-[24px] border border-slate-200 bg-white p-5"
   966	                      >
   967	                        <div className="flex flex-col gap-4 sm:flex-row sm:items-start sm:justify-between">
   968	                          <div>
   969	                            <div className="inline-flex rounded-full bg-orange-50 px-3 py-1 text-xs font-semibold text-orange-700">
   970	                              Day {item.day}
   971	                            </div>
   972	                            <h3 className="mt-3 text-lg font-semibold text-slate-950">
   973	                              {item.title}
   974	                            </h3>
   975	                            <p className="mt-1 text-sm font-medium text-sky-700">
   976	                              {item.city}
   977	                            </p>
   978	                            <p className="mt-3 text-sm leading-6 text-slate-600">
   979	                              {item.description}
   980	                            </p>
   981	                          </div>
   982	
   983	                          <div className="flex gap-2">
   984	                            <button
   985	                              type="button"
   986	                              onClick={() => handleCustomizePackage(detailPackage.id)}
   987	                              className="rounded-full border border-slate-200 bg-white px-4 py-2 text-xs font-semibold text-slate-700"
   988	                            >
   989	                              Modify day
   990	                            </button>
   991	                          </div>
   992	                        </div>
   993	
   994	                        <div className="mt-4 grid gap-2 text-sm text-slate-700 sm:grid-cols-2">
   995	                          {item.transfer ? <InfoBullet text={item.transfer} /> : null}
   996	                          {item.hotel ? <InfoBullet text={item.hotel} /> : null}
   997	                          {item.activities?.map((activity) => (
   998	                            <InfoBullet key={activity} text={activity} />
   999	                          ))}
  1000	                          {item.meals?.map((meal) => (
  1001	                            <InfoBullet key={meal} text={meal} />
  1002	                          ))}
  1003	                        </div>
  1004	                      </div>
  1005	                    ))}
  1006	                  </div>
  1007	                </div>
  1008	              </div>
  1009	
  1010	              <aside className="border-l border-slate-200 bg-slate-50 px-5 py-5">
  1011	                <div className="rounded-[24px] border border-slate-200 bg-white p-5">
  1012	                  <p className="text-xs font-semibold uppercase tracking-[0.18em] text-sky-600">
  1013	                    Current estimate
  1014	                  </p>
  1015	                  <p className="mt-3 text-3xl font-semibold text-slate-950">
  1016	                    {formatINR(detailPackage.pricing.totalPrice)}
  1017	                  </p>
  1018	                  <p className="mt-1 text-sm text-slate-500">
  1019	                    {formatINR(detailPackage.pricing.pricePerPerson)} / person
  1020	                  </p>
  1021	
  1022	                  <div className="mt-4 space-y-3">
  1023	                    <SummaryRow label="Departure" value={formatLongDate(departureDate)} />
  1024	                    <SummaryRow label="Guests" value={`${totalTravellers}`} />
  1025	                    <SummaryRow label="Rooms" value={`${rooms}`} />
  1026	                  </div>
  1027	
  1028	                  <div className="mt-5 grid gap-2">
  1029	                    <button
  1030	                      type="button"
  1031	                      onClick={() => {
  1032	                        handleSelectPackage(detailPackage.id);
  1033	                        handleCloseDetail();
  1034	                      }}
  1035	                      className="rounded-full bg-slate-950 px-4 py-3 text-sm font-semibold text-white transition hover:bg-slate-800"
  1036	                    >
  1037	                      Choose this package
  1038	                    </button>
  1039	                    <button
  1040	                      type="button"
  1041	                      onClick={() => handleCustomizePackage(detailPackage.id)}
  1042	                      className="rounded-full border border-sky-200 bg-sky-50 px-4 py-3 text-sm font-semibold text-sky-700 transition hover:bg-sky-100"
  1043	                    >
  1044	                      Customize this package
  1045	                    </button>
  1046	                  </div>
  1047	                </div>
  1048	              </aside>
  1049	            </div>
  1050	          </div>
  1051	        </div>
  1052	      ) : null}
  1053	    </div>
  1054	  );
  1055	}

  1057	function SearchField({
  1058	  label,
  1059	  value,
  1060	  onChange,
  1061	  type = "text",
  1062	  min,
  1063	  icon,
  1064	}: {
  1065	  label: string;
  1066	  value: string;
  1067	  onChange: (value: string) => void;
  1068	  type?: "text" | "date";
  1069	  min?: string;
  1070	  icon: React.ReactNode;
  1071	}) {
  1072	  return (
  1073	    <label className="rounded-2xl bg-white/10 px-4 py-3 text-white">
  1074	      <span className="mb-1 flex items-center gap-2 text-[11px] font-semibold uppercase tracking-[0.18em] text-sky-100">
  1075	        {icon}
  1076	        {label}
  1077	      </span>
  1078	      <input
  1079	        type={type}
  1080	        value={value}
  1081	        min={min}
  1082	        onChange={(e) => onChange(e.target.value)}
  1083	        className="w-full bg-transparent text-base font-medium text-white outline-none [color-scheme:dark]"
  1084	      />
  1085	    </label>
  1086	  );
  1087	}
  1088	
  1089	function GuestsField({
  1090	  adults,
  1091	  children,
  1092	  rooms,
  1093	  setAdults,
  1094	  setChildren,
  1095	  setRooms,
  1096	}: {
  1097	  adults: number;
  1098	  children: number;
  1099	  rooms: number;
  1100	  setAdults: (value: number) => void;
  1101	  setChildren: (value: number) => void;
  1102	  setRooms: (value: number) => void;
  1103	}) {
  1104	  return (
  1105	    <div className="rounded-2xl bg-white/10 px-4 py-3 text-white">
  1106	      <div className="mb-1 flex items-center gap-2 text-[11px] font-semibold uppercase tracking-[0.18em] text-sky-100">
  1107	        <Users className="h-4 w-4" />
  1108	        Rooms & Guests
  1109	      </div>
  1110	      <div className="grid grid-cols-3 gap-2">
  1111	        <CounterMini
  1112	          label="A"
  1113	          value={adults}
  1114	          onMinus={() => setAdults(clampMinimum(adults - 1, 1))}
  1115	          onPlus={() => setAdults(adults + 1)}
  1116	        />
  1117	        <CounterMini
  1118	          label="C"
  1119	          value={children}
  1120	          onMinus={() => setChildren(clampMinimum(children - 1, 0))}
  1121	          onPlus={() => setChildren(children + 1)}
  1122	        />
  1123	        <CounterMini
  1124	          label="R"
  1125	          value={rooms}
  1126	          onMinus={() => setRooms(clampMinimum(rooms - 1, 1))}
  1127	          onPlus={() => setRooms(rooms + 1)}
  1128	        />
  1129	      </div>
  1130	    </div>
  1131	  );
  1132	}
  1133	
  1134	function CounterMini({
  1135	  label,
  1136	  value,
  1137	  onMinus,
  1138	  onPlus,
  1139	}: {
  1140	  label: string;
  1141	  value: number;
  1142	  onMinus: () => void;
  1143	  onPlus: () => void;
  1144	}) {
  1145	  return (
  1146	    <div className="rounded-xl bg-white/10 px-2 py-2">
  1147	      <div className="mb-1 text-center text-[10px] font-semibold uppercase tracking-[0.18em] text-sky-100">
  1148	        {label}
  1149	      </div>
  1150	      <div className="flex items-center justify-between gap-1">
  1151	        <button
  1152	          type="button"
  1153	          onClick={onMinus}
  1154	          className="inline-flex h-6 w-6 items-center justify-center rounded-full bg-white/10"
  1155	        >
  1156	          <Minus className="h-3 w-3" />
  1157	        </button>
  1158	        <span className="text-sm font-semibold">{value}</span>
  1159	        <button
  1160	          type="button"
  1161	          onClick={onPlus}
  1162	          className="inline-flex h-6 w-6 items-center justify-center rounded-full bg-white/10"
  1163	        >
  1164	          <Plus className="h-3 w-3" />
  1165	        </button>
  1166	      </div>
  1167	    </div>
  1168	  );
  1169	}
  1170	
  1171	function ModeCard({
  1172	  active,
  1173	  title,
  1174	  description,
  1175	  onClick,
  1176	  icon,
  1177	}: {
  1178	  active: boolean;
  1179	  title: string;
  1180	  description: string;
  1181	  onClick: () => void;
  1182	  icon: React.ReactNode;
  1183	}) {
  1184	  return (
  1185	    <button
  1186	      type="button"
  1187	      onClick={onClick}
  1188	      className={`rounded-[28px] border p-5 text-left transition ${
  1189	        active
  1190	          ? "border-sky-400 bg-sky-50 shadow-sm"
  1191	          : "border-slate-200 bg-white hover:border-slate-300"
  1192	      }`}
  1193	    >
  1194	      <div className="flex items-center gap-3">
  1195	        <div className="rounded-full bg-slate-100 p-3 text-slate-700">{icon}</div>
  1196	        <div>
  1197	          <p className="text-lg font-semibold text-slate-950">{title}</p>
  1198	          <p className="text-sm text-slate-500">{description}</p>
  1199	        </div>
  1200	      </div>
  1201	    </button>
  1202	  );
  1203	}

  1205	function FactPill({ label }: { label: string }) {
  1206	  return (
  1207	    <div className="rounded-full border border-slate-200 bg-slate-50 px-3 py-2 text-center text-xs font-medium text-slate-700">
  1208	      {label}
  1209	    </div>
  1210	  );
  1211	}
  1212	
  1213	function InfoBullet({ text }: { text: string }) {
  1214	  return (
  1215	    <div className="flex items-start gap-2">
  1216	      <span className="mt-1 h-1.5 w-1.5 rounded-full bg-slate-400" />
  1217	      <span>{text}</span>
  1218	    </div>
  1219	  );
  1220	}
  1221	
  1222	function SummaryRow({ label, value }: { label: string; value: string }) {
  1223	  return (
  1224	    <div className="flex items-center justify-between rounded-2xl border border-slate-100 bg-white px-4 py-3">
  1225	      <span className="text-slate-500">{label}</span>
  1226	      <span className="text-right font-medium text-slate-900">{value}</span>
  1227	    </div>
  1228	  );
  1229	}
  1230	
  1231	function DetailInfoCard({ label, value }: { label: string; value: string }) {
  1232	  return (
  1233	    <div className="rounded-[22px] border border-slate-200 bg-white p-4">
  1234	      <p className="text-xs font-semibold uppercase tracking-[0.18em] text-slate-400">
  1235	        {label}
  1236	      </p>
  1237	      <p className="mt-2 text-sm font-semibold text-slate-950">{value}</p>
  1238	    </div>
  1239	  );
  1240	}

     1	"use client";

     5	type Props = {
     6	  value: string;
     7	  onChange: (value: string) => void;
     8	};
     9	
    10	export function TripStyleChips({ value, onChange }: Props) {
    11	  return (
    12	    <div className="rounded-[28px] border border-slate-200 bg-white p-4 shadow-sm">
    13	      <div className="mb-4">
    14	        <p className="text-sm font-semibold text-slate-950">What kind of trip do you want?</p>
    15	        <p className="text-xs text-slate-500">Pick the vibe that fits your trip best</p>
    16	      </div>
    17	
    18	      <div className="flex flex-wrap gap-2">
    19	        {tripStyles.map((item) => {
    20	          const active = value === item;
    21	
    22	          return (
    23	            <button
    24	              key={item}
    25	              type="button"
    26	              onClick={() => onChange(item)}
    27	              className={`rounded-full px-4 py-2 text-sm font-medium transition ${
    28	                active
    29	                  ? "bg-sky-500 text-white"
    30	                  : "bg-slate-100 text-slate-700 hover:bg-slate-200"
    31	              }`}
    32	            >
    33	              {item}
    34	            </button>
    35	          );
    36	        })}
    37	      </div>
    38	    </div>
    39	  );
    40	}===== END: src/components/trip-builder/trip-style-chips.tsx =====

===== START: src/lib/helpers/format.ts =====
     1	export function formatCurrency(amount: number): string {
     2	  return new Intl.NumberFormat("en-IN", {
     3	    style: "currency",
     4	    currency: "INR",
     5	    maximumFractionDigits: 0,
     6	  }).format(amount);
     7	}
     8	
     9	export function formatDateRange(
    10	  startDate?: string | null,
    11	  endDate?: string | null
    12	): string {
    13	  if (!startDate || !endDate) return "Dates to be selected";
    14	
    15	  const start = new Date(startDate);
    16	  const end = new Date(endDate);
    17	
    18	  const formattedStart = start.toLocaleDateString("en-IN", {
    19	    day: "numeric",
    20	    month: "short",
    21	  });
    22	
    23	  const formattedEnd = end.toLocaleDateString("en-IN", {
    24	    day: "numeric",
    25	    month: "short",
    26	    year: "numeric",
    27	  });
    28	
    29	  return `${formattedStart} - ${formattedEnd}`;
    30	}
    31	
    32	export function formatTravelerCount(adults = 0, children = 0): string {
    33	  const parts: string[] = [];
    34	
    35	  if (adults > 0) {
    36	    parts.push(`${adults} Adult${adults > 1 ? "s" : ""}`);
    37	  }
    38	
    39	  if (children > 0) {
    40	    parts.push(`${children} Child${children > 1 ? "ren" : ""}`);
    41	  }
    42	
    43	  if (parts.length === 0) {
    44	    return "No travelers selected";
    45	  }
    46	
    47	  return parts.join(", ");
    48	}===== END: src/lib/helpers/format.ts =====

===== START: src/lib/helpers/pricing.ts =====
     1	import { transfers, type Transfer, type TransferPurpose } from "@/data/transfers";
     2	import type { Hotel } from "@/data/hotels";
     3	
     4	export type PricedItem = {
     5	  id: string;
     6	  price?: number;
     7	  quantity?: number;
     8	};
     9	
    10	export type PassengerMix = {
    11	  adults: number;
    12	  children: number;
    13	};
    14	
    15	export function getTotalPassengers({ adults, children }: PassengerMix): number {
    16	  return Math.max(0, adults) + Math.max(0, children);
    17	}
    18	
    19	export function calculateNights(checkIn?: string, checkOut?: string): number {
    20	  if (!checkIn || !checkOut) return 0;
    21	
    22	  const start = new Date(checkIn);
    23	  const end = new Date(checkOut);
    24	
    25	  if (Number.isNaN(start.getTime()) || Number.isNaN(end.getTime())) return 0;
    26	
    27	  const diffMs = end.getTime() - start.getTime();
    28	  const nights = Math.floor(diffMs / (1000 * 60 * 60 * 24));
    29	
    30	  return nights > 0 ? nights : 0;
    31	}
    32	
    33	export function getRecommendedTransfer(params: {
    34	  adults: number;
    35	  children: number;
    36	  purpose: TransferPurpose;
    37	  destinationId?: string;
    38	  preferPremium?: boolean;
    39	}): Transfer | null {
    40	  const totalPax = getTotalPassengers({
    41	    adults: params.adults,
    42	    children: params.children,
    43	  });
    44	
    45	  const destinationId = params.destinationId ?? "dest-bangkok";
    46	
    47	  const matching = transfers.filter(
    48	    (item) =>
    49	      item.isActive &&
    50	      item.purpose === params.purpose &&
    51	      item.destinationIds.includes(destinationId) &&
    52	      totalPax >= item.minPax &&
    53	      totalPax <= item.maxPax
    54	  );
    55	
    56	  if (!matching.length) return null;
    57	
    58	  if (params.preferPremium) {
    59	    const premium = matching.find((item) => item.serviceType === "premium-private");
    60	    if (premium) return premium;
    61	  }
    62	
    63	  const preferredOrder = ["private", "premium-private", "shared"];
    64	
    65	  const sorted = [...matching].sort((a, b) => {
    66	    const serviceScore =
    67	      preferredOrder.indexOf(a.serviceType) - preferredOrder.indexOf(b.serviceType);
    68	
    69	    if (serviceScore !== 0) return serviceScore;
    70	
    71	    const vehicleOrder = ["sedan", "suv", "van", "mini-coach", "seat-in-coach"];
    72	    return vehicleOrder.indexOf(a.vehicleClass) - vehicleOrder.indexOf(b.vehicleClass);
    73	  });
    74	
    75	  return sorted[0] ?? null;
    76	}
    77	
    78	export function calculateHotelTotal(params: {
    79	  hotel: Hotel | null;
    80	  nights: number;
    81	  rooms: number;
    82	}): number {
    83	  if (!params.hotel || params.nights <= 0 || params.rooms <= 0) return 0;
    84	
    85	  return params.hotel.nightlyRate * params.nights * params.rooms;
    86	}
    87	
    88	export function calculateHotelMargin(params: {
    89	  hotel: Hotel | null;
    90	  nights: number;
    91	  rooms: number;
    92	}): number {
    93	  if (!params.hotel || params.nights <= 0 || params.rooms <= 0) return 0;
    94	
    95	  return params.hotel.margin * params.nights * params.rooms;
    96	}
    97	
    98	export function calculateSightseeingTotal(
    99	  selectedItems: Array<PricedItem>,
   100	  passengerCount = 1
   101	): number {
   102	  return selectedItems.reduce((sum, item) => {
   103	    const quantity = item.quantity ?? passengerCount;
   104	    return sum + (item.price ?? 0) * quantity;
   105	  }, 0);
   106	}
   107	
   108	export function calculateMealsTotal(
   109	  selectedItems: Array<PricedItem>,
   110	  passengerCount = 1
   111	): number {
   112	  return selectedItems.reduce((sum, item) => {
   113	    const quantity = item.quantity ?? passengerCount;
   114	    return sum + (item.price ?? 0) * quantity;
   115	  }, 0);
   116	}
   117	
   118	export function calculateTransferTotal(params: {
   119	  arrivalTransfer?: Transfer | null;
   120	  departureTransfer?: Transfer | null;
   121	  localTransfer?: Transfer | null;
   122	}): number {
   123	  return (
   124	    (params.arrivalTransfer?.price ?? 0) +
   125	    (params.departureTransfer?.price ?? 0) +
   126	    (params.localTransfer?.price ?? 0)
   127	  );
   128	}
   129	
   130	export function calculateTransferMargin(params: {
   131	  arrivalTransfer?: Transfer | null;
   132	  departureTransfer?: Transfer | null;
   133	  localTransfer?: Transfer | null;
   134	}): number {
   135	  return (
   136	    (params.arrivalTransfer?.margin ?? 0) +
   137	    (params.departureTransfer?.margin ?? 0) +
   138	    (params.localTransfer?.margin ?? 0)
   139	  );
   140	}
   141	
   142	export function calculateBasePackagePrice(basePrice: number): number {
   143	  return basePrice > 0 ? basePrice : 0;
   144	}
   145	
   146	export function calculateHotelDelta(delta: number): number {
   147	  return delta > 0 ? delta : 0;
   148	}
   149	
   150	export function calculateGrandTotal(params: {
   151	  basePrice?: number;
   152	  hotelTotal?: number;
   153	  hotelDelta?: number;
   154	  transferTotal?: number;
   155	  sightseeingTotal?: number;
   156	  mealsTotal?: number;
   157	  serviceFee?: number;
   158	}): number {
   159	  return (
   160	    (params.basePrice ?? 0) +
   161	    (params.hotelTotal ?? 0) +
   162	    (params.hotelDelta ?? 0) +
   163	    (params.transferTotal ?? 0) +
   164	    (params.sightseeingTotal ?? 0) +
   165	    (params.mealsTotal ?? 0) +
   166	    (params.serviceFee ?? 0)
   167	  );
   168	}
   169	
   170	export function calculateTripGrandTotal(params: {
   171	  packageBasePrice?: number;
   172	  hotel: Hotel | null;
   173	  nights: number;
   174	  rooms: number;
   175	  arrivalTransfer?: Transfer | null;
   176	  departureTransfer?: Transfer | null;
   177	  localTransfer?: Transfer | null;
   178	  sightseeingItems?: Array<PricedItem>;
   179	  mealItems?: Array<PricedItem>;
   180	  passengerCount: number;
   181	  serviceFee?: number;
   182	  includeStandaloneHotel?: boolean;
   183	}): number {
   184	  const hotelTotal = params.includeStandaloneHotel
   185	    ? calculateHotelTotal({
   186	        hotel: params.hotel,
   187	        nights: params.nights,
   188	        rooms: params.rooms,
   189	      })
   190	    : 0;
   191	
   192	  const transferTotal = calculateTransferTotal({
   193	    arrivalTransfer: params.arrivalTransfer,
   194	    departureTransfer: params.departureTransfer,
   195	    localTransfer: params.localTransfer,
   196	  });
   197	
   198	  const sightseeingTotal = calculateSightseeingTotal(
   199	    params.sightseeingItems ?? [],
   200	    params.passengerCount
   201	  );
   202	
   203	  const mealsTotal = calculateMealsTotal(params.mealItems ?? [], params.passengerCount);
   204	
   205	  return calculateGrandTotal({
   206	    basePrice: params.packageBasePrice ?? 0,
   207	    hotelTotal,
   208	    transferTotal,
   209	    sightseeingTotal,
   210	    mealsTotal,
   211	    serviceFee: params.serviceFee ?? 0,
   212	  });
   213	}===== END: src/lib/helpers/pricing.ts =====

===== START: src/lib/helpers/recommendation.ts =====
     1	import type { Hotel, HotelTag } from "@/data/hotels";
     2	import { hotels } from "@/data/hotels";
     3	import {
     4	  getRecommendedTransfer as getRecommendedTransferFromPricing,
     5	} from "@/lib/helpers/pricing";

     8	export type PackageLike = {
     9	  id: string;
    10	  title: string;
    11	  basePrice: number;
    12	  popularityScore?: number;
    13	  marginScore?: number;
    14	  budgetFitScore?: number;
    15	  tripMoodFitScore?: number;
    16	  recommendedLabel?: string;
    17	};
    18	
    19	export type TripDayType =
    20	  | "arrival"
    21	  | "full-day"
    22	  | "relaxed"
    23	  | "departure";
    24	
    25	export type DayPlan = {
    26	  dayNumber: number;
    27	  label: string;
    28	  dayType: TripDayType;
    29	  allowedTimeSlots: Array<"morning" | "afternoon" | "evening" | "night">;
    30	  notes: string[];
    31	};
    32	
    33	type BuildTripDayParams = {
    34	  nights: number;
    35	  arrivalTimeSlot?: "early-morning" | "morning" | "afternoon" | "evening" | "night";
    36	  departureTimeSlot?: "morning" | "afternoon" | "evening" | "night";
    37	};
    38	
    39	export function getRecommendedPackages(packages: PackageLike[]): PackageLike[] {
    40	  return [...packages]
    41	    .sort((a, b) => {
    42	      const scoreA =
    43	        (a.popularityScore || 0) +
    44	        (a.marginScore || 0) +
    45	        (a.budgetFitScore || 0) +
    46	        (a.tripMoodFitScore || 0);
    47	
    48	      const scoreB =
    49	        (b.popularityScore || 0) +
    50	        (b.marginScore || 0) +
    51	        (b.budgetFitScore || 0) +
    52	        (b.tripMoodFitScore || 0);
    53	
    54	      return scoreB - scoreA;
    55	    })
    56	    .slice(0, 6);
    57	}
    58	
    59	export function getPackageBadge(pkg: PackageLike): string {
    60	  if (pkg.recommendedLabel) return pkg.recommendedLabel;
    61	  if ((pkg.popularityScore || 0) >= 9) return "Most Booked";
    62	  if ((pkg.budgetFitScore || 0) >= 9) return "Best Value";
    63	  if ((pkg.tripMoodFitScore || 0) >= 9) return "Great Match for You";
    64	  if ((pkg.marginScore || 0) >= 9) return "Top Pick";
    65	  return "Popular Choice";
    66	}
    67	
    68	export function getRecommendationReason(pkg: PackageLike): string {
    69	  if ((pkg.tripMoodFitScore || 0) >= 9) {
    70	    return "This package strongly matches your selected trip mood.";
    71	  }
    72	
    73	  if ((pkg.budgetFitScore || 0) >= 9) {
    74	    return "This package gives a strong balance of experience and value.";
    75	  }
    76	
    77	  if ((pkg.popularityScore || 0) >= 9) {
    78	    return "Travelers choose this package often for its overall convenience.";
    79	  }
    80	
    81	  if ((pkg.marginScore || 0) >= 9) {
    82	    return "This option includes premium value additions and smoother experience.";
    83	  }
    84	
    85	  return "This is a solid all-round option for your travel plan.";
    86	}
    87	
    88	export function buildTripDayPlans(params: BuildTripDayParams): DayPlan[] {
    89	  const totalDays = Math.max(1, params.nights + 1);
    90	  const plans: DayPlan[] = [];
    91	
    92	  for (let day = 1; day <= totalDays; day += 1) {
    93	    if (day === 1) {
    94	      const notes = ["Arrival day should stay light and practical."];
    95	
    96	      if (
    97	        params.arrivalTimeSlot === "early-morning" ||
    98	        params.arrivalTimeSlot === "morning"
    99	      ) {
   100	        notes.push("Avoid strict early-entry sightseeing after overnight flights.");
   101	        plans.push({
   102	          dayNumber: day,
   103	          label: "Arrival Day",
   104	          dayType: "arrival",
   105	          allowedTimeSlots: ["afternoon", "evening", "night"],
   106	          notes,
   107	        });
   108	      } else {
   109	        notes.push("Keep the plan flexible around check-in and rest.");
   110	        plans.push({
   111	          dayNumber: day,
   112	          label: "Arrival Day",
   113	          dayType: "arrival",
   114	          allowedTimeSlots: ["evening", "night"],
   115	          notes,
   116	        });
   117	      }
   118	
   119	      continue;
   120	    }
   121	
   122	    if (day === totalDays) {
   123	      const notes = ["Departure day should stay operationally safe and buffer-friendly."];
   124	
   125	      if (params.departureTimeSlot === "morning") {
   126	        notes.push("Do not recommend major sightseeing.");
   127	        plans.push({
   128	          dayNumber: day,
   129	          label: "Departure Day",
   130	          dayType: "departure",
   131	          allowedTimeSlots: [],
   132	          notes,
   133	        });
   134	      } else if (params.departureTimeSlot === "afternoon") {
   135	        notes.push("Only short and nearby activities should be shown.");
   136	        plans.push({
   137	          dayNumber: day,
   138	          label: "Departure Day",
   139	          dayType: "departure",
   140	          allowedTimeSlots: ["morning"],
   141	          notes,
   142	        });
   143	      } else {
   144	        notes.push("A light half-day plan may be possible before airport transfer.");
   145	        plans.push({
   146	          dayNumber: day,
   147	          label: "Departure Day",
   148	          dayType: "departure",
   149	          allowedTimeSlots: ["morning", "afternoon"],
   150	          notes,
   151	        });
   152	      }
   153	
   154	      continue;
   155	    }
   156	
   157	    plans.push({
   158	      dayNumber: day,
   159	      label: `Day ${day}`,
   160	      dayType: "full-day",
   161	      allowedTimeSlots: ["morning", "afternoon", "evening"],
   162	      notes: ["Best suited for primary sightseeing and main city experiences."],
   163	    });
   164	  }
   165	
   166	  return plans;
   167	}
   168	
   169	export function isEarlyStartRestrictedOnArrival(
   170	  arrivalTimeSlot?: "early-morning" | "morning" | "afternoon" | "evening" | "night"
   171	): boolean {
   172	  return arrivalTimeSlot === "early-morning" || arrivalTimeSlot === "morning";
   173	}
   174	
   175	export function getHotelTagMatches(tripStyle: string, travellingWith: string): HotelTag[] {
   176	  const normalizedStyle = tripStyle.toLowerCase();
   177	  const normalizedGroup = travellingWith.toLowerCase();
   178	
   179	  const tags = new Set<HotelTag>();
   180	
   181	  if (normalizedStyle.includes("lux")) tags.add("luxury");
   182	  if (normalizedStyle.includes("shop")) tags.add("shopping");
   183	  if (normalizedStyle.includes("night")) tags.add("nightlife");
   184	  if (normalizedStyle.includes("mixed")) tags.add("first-timer");
   185	  if (normalizedStyle.includes("comfort")) tags.add("premium-comfort");
   186	
   187	  if (normalizedGroup.includes("couple")) tags.add("couple");
   188	  if (normalizedGroup.includes("family")) tags.add("family");
   189	  if (normalizedGroup.includes("friend")) tags.add("nightlife");
   190	
   191	  if (tags.size === 0) {
   192	    tags.add("first-timer");
   193	    tags.add("value");
   194	  }
   195	
   196	  return [...tags];
   197	}
   198	
   199	export function getRecommendedHotels(params: {
   200	  destinationId?: string;
   201	  budget?: string;
   202	  category?: "3 Star" | "4 Star" | "5 Star";
   203	  tripStyle?: string;
   204	  travellingWith?: string;
   205	  limit?: number;
   206	}): Hotel[] {
   207	  const destinationId = params.destinationId ?? "dest-bangkok";
   208	  const requestedTags = getHotelTagMatches(
   209	    params.tripStyle ?? "Mixed",
   210	    params.travellingWith ?? "Couple"
   211	  );
   212	
   213	  return hotels
   214	    .filter(
   215	      (hotel) =>
   216	        hotel.isActive &&
   217	        hotel.destinationId === destinationId &&
   218	        (!params.category || hotel.category === params.category)
   219	    )
   220	    .map((hotel) => {
   221	      const tagScore = hotel.tags.reduce(
   222	        (sum, tag) => sum + (requestedTags.includes(tag) ? 2 : 0),
   223	        0
   224	      );
   225	
   226	      const budgetScore =
   227	        params.budget === "Economy" && hotel.category === "3 Star"
   228	          ? 3
   229	          : params.budget === "Comfort" && hotel.category === "4 Star"
   230	          ? 3
   231	          : (params.budget === "Premium" || params.budget === "Luxury") &&
   232	            hotel.category === "5 Star"
   233	          ? 3
   234	          : 0;
   235	
   236	      const score = tagScore + budgetScore + hotel.rating;
   237	
   238	      return { hotel, score };
   239	    })
   240	    .sort((a, b) => b.score - a.score)
   241	    .slice(0, params.limit ?? 6)
   242	    .map((item) => item.hotel);
   243	}
   244	
   245	export function getRecommendedTransfer(params: {
   246	  adults: number;
   247	  children: number;
   248	  purpose: TransferPurpose;
   249	  destinationId?: string;
   250	  budget?: string;
   251	  travellingWith?: string;
   252	}): Transfer | null {
   253	  const preferPremium =
   254	    params.budget === "Luxury" ||
   255	    params.budget === "Premium" ||
   256	    (params.travellingWith ?? "").toLowerCase().includes("couple");
   257	
   258	  return getRecommendedTransferFromPricing({
   259	    adults: params.adults,
   260	    children: params.children,
   261	    purpose: params.purpose,
   262	    destinationId: params.destinationId ?? "dest-bangkok",
   263	    preferPremium,
   264	  });
   265	}===== END: src/lib/helpers/recommendation.ts =====

   134	    estimatedTransferTotal?: number;
   135	    estimatedSightseeingTotal?: number;
   136	    estimatedMealsTotal?: number;
   137	    estimatedGrandTotal?: number;
   138	  }) => void;
   139	  setBookingId: (value: string) => void;
   140	  resetTrip: () => void;
   141	};
   142	
   143	const initialAiMessages: ChatMessage[] = [
   144	  {
   145	    id: "ai-1",
   146	    role: "assistant",
   147	    text: "Tell me the kind of holiday you want and I will guide you toward the best trip style.",
   148	  },
   149	  {
   150	    id: "ai-2",
   151	    role: "assistant",
   152	    text: "You can mention things like family trip, nightlife, shopping, comfort, luxury, or a relaxed pace.",
   153	  },
   154	];
   155	
   156	const initialState: Omit<
   157	  TripBuilderState,
   158	  | "setTripDetails"
   159	  | "setSelectedMode"
   160	  | "setBudget"
   161	  | "setMood"
   162	  | "setTravelStyle"

   176	  | "resetAiChat"

   179	  | "setHotelCategory"

   188	  | "setRoomPreference"

   191	  | "setBookingId"
   192	  | "resetTrip"
   193	> = {

   258	
   259	export const useTripBuilderStore = create<TripBuilderState>((set) => ({
   260	  ...initialState,
   261	
   262	  setTripDetails: (payload) =>
   263	    set((state) => ({
   264	      ...state,
   265	      ...payload,
   266	    })),
   267	
   268	  setSelectedMode: (mode) =>
   269	    set(() => ({
   270	      selectedMode: mode,
   271	    })),
   272	
   273	  setBudget: (value) =>
   274	    set(() => ({
   275	      budget: value,
   276	    })),
   277	
   278	  setMood: (value) =>
   279	    set(() => ({
   280	      mood: value,
   281	    })),
   282	
   283	  setTravelStyle: (value) =>
   284	    set(() => ({
   285	      travelStyle: value,
   286	    })),
   287	
   288	  setTravellingWith: (value) =>
   289	    set(() => ({
   290	      travellingWith: value,
   291	    })),
   292	
   293	  setPriority: (value) =>
   294	    set(() => ({
   295	      priority: value,
   296	    })),
   297	
   298	  setSpecialRequest: (value) =>
   299	    set(() => ({
   300	      specialRequest: value,
   301	    })),
   302	
   303	  setSegments: (segments) =>
   304	    set(() => ({
   305	      segments,
   306	    })),
   307	
   308	  addSegment: () =>
   309	    set((state) => ({
   310	      segments: [
   311	        ...state.segments,
   312	        {
   313	          id: `segment-${Date.now()}`,
   314	          city: "",
   315	          destinationId: "",
   316	          checkIn: "",
   317	          checkOut: "",
   318	        },
   319	      ],
   320	    })),
   321	
   322	  updateSegment: (id, values) =>
   323	    set((state) => ({
   324	      segments: state.segments.map((segment) => {
   325	        if (segment.id !== id) return segment;
   326	
   327	        const next = { ...segment, ...values };
   328	
   329	        if (
   330	          next.checkIn &&
   331	          next.checkOut &&
   332	          new Date(next.checkOut).getTime() <= new Date(next.checkIn).getTime()
   333	        ) {
   334	          next.checkOut = "";
   335	        }
   336	
   337	        return next;
   338	      }),
   339	    })),
   340	
   341	  removeSegment: (id) =>
   342	    set((state) => ({
   343	      segments:
   344	        state.segments.length <= 1
   345	          ? state.segments
   346	          : state.segments.filter((segment) => segment.id !== id),
   347	    })),
   348	
   349	  setArrivalTimeSlot: (value) =>
   350	    set(() => ({
   351	      arrivalTimeSlot: value,
   352	    })),
   353	
   354	  setDepartureTimeSlot: (value) =>
   355	    set(() => ({
   356	      departureTimeSlot: value,
   357	    })),
   358	
   359	  setTravelers: ({ adults, children, rooms }) =>
   360	    set((state) => ({
   361	      adults: adults ?? state.adults,
   362	      children: children ?? state.children,
   363	      rooms: rooms ?? state.rooms,
   364	    })),
   365	
   366	  togglePreference: (value) =>
   367	    set((state) => ({
   368	      specialPreferences: state.specialPreferences.includes(value)
   369	        ? state.specialPreferences.filter((item) => item !== value)
   370	        : [...state.specialPreferences, value],
   371	    })),
   372	
   373	  setAiPrompt: (value) =>
   374	    set(() => ({
   375	      aiPrompt: value,
   376	    })),
   377	
   378	  addAiChatMessage: (message) =>
   379	    set((state) => ({
   380	      aiChatMessages: [...state.aiChatMessages, message],
   381	    })),
   382	
   383	  resetAiChat: () =>
   384	    set(() => ({
   385	      aiChatMessages: initialAiMessages,
   386	    })),
   387	
   388	  selectPackage: ({ selectedPackageId, selectedPackageTitle, selectedPackagePrice }) =>
   389	    set(() => ({
   390	      selectedPackageId,
   391	      selectedPackageTitle,
   392	      selectedPackagePrice,
   393	    })),
   394	
   395	  setSelectedHotelId: (value) =>
   396	    set(() => ({
   397	      selectedHotelId: value,
   398	    })),
   399	
   400	  setHotelCategory: (value) =>
   401	    set(() => ({
   402	      hotelCategory: value,
   403	    })),
   404	
   405	  setSelectedArrivalTransferId: (value) =>
   406	    set(() => ({
   407	      selectedArrivalTransferId: value,
   408	    })),
   409	
   410	  setSelectedDepartureTransferId: (value) =>
   411	    set(() => ({
   412	      selectedDepartureTransferId: value,
   413	    })),
   414	
   415	  setSelectedLocalTransferId: (value) =>
   416	    set(() => ({
   417	      selectedLocalTransferId: value,
   418	    })),
   419	
   420	  setTransferType: (value) =>
   421	    set(() => ({
   422	      transferType: value,
   423	    })),
   424	
   425	  toggleSightseeing: (value) =>
   426	    set((state) => ({
   427	      selectedSightseeingIds: state.selectedSightseeingIds.includes(value)
   428	        ? state.selectedSightseeingIds.filter((item) => item !== value)
   429	        : [...state.selectedSightseeingIds, value],
   430	    })),
   431	
   432	  toggleMeal: (value) =>
   433	    set((state) => ({
   434	      selectedMealIds: state.selectedMealIds.includes(value)
   435	        ? state.selectedMealIds.filter((item) => item !== value)
   436	        : [...state.selectedMealIds, value],
   437	    })),
   438	
   439	  toggleExtra: (value) =>
   440	    set((state) => ({
   441	      selectedExtras: state.selectedExtras.includes(value)
   442	        ? state.selectedExtras.filter((item) => item !== value)
   443	        : [...state.selectedExtras, value],
   444	    })),
   445	
   446	  toggleAddOn: (value) =>
   447	    set((state) => ({
   448	      selectedAddOns: state.selectedAddOns.includes(value)
   449	        ? state.selectedAddOns.filter((item) => item !== value)
   450	        : [...state.selectedAddOns, value],
   451	    })),
   452	
   453	  setRoomPreference: (value) =>
   454	    set(() => ({
   455	      roomPreference: value,
   456	    })),
   457	
   458	  setDayPlans: (plans) =>
   459	    set(() => ({
   460	      dayPlans: plans,
   461	    })),
   462	
   463	  setTotals: (payload) =>
   464	    set((state) => ({
   465	      estimatedHotelTotal: payload.estimatedHotelTotal ?? state.estimatedHotelTotal,
   466	      estimatedTransferTotal: payload.estimatedTransferTotal ?? state.estimatedTransferTotal,
   467	      estimatedSightseeingTotal:
   468	        payload.estimatedSightseeingTotal ?? state.estimatedSightseeingTotal,
   469	      estimatedMealsTotal: payload.estimatedMealsTotal ?? state.estimatedMealsTotal,
   470	      estimatedGrandTotal: payload.estimatedGrandTotal ?? state.estimatedGrandTotal,
   471	    })),
   472	
   473	  setBookingId: (value) =>
   474	    set(() => ({
   475	      bookingId: value,
   476	    })),
   477	
   478	  resetTrip: () =>
   479	    set(() => ({
   480	      ...initialState,
   481	      aiChatMessages: initialAiMessages,
   482	    })),
   483	}));===== END: src/store/useTripBuilderStore.ts =====
